International Commercial Telegram: Reuters Special Commercial Telegram, August 1st 31

Gold and Silver

The price of gold in London today was 138 shillings and 8 pence, down 1 penny and 1/2.

The Mount Lyell market was quiet today. The opening price for December futures was 44.73/45.05, the same as yesterday.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was quite active this morning, with the pound sterling slightly weaker against the U.S. dollar. The opening exchange rate for British-American was $5.01 7, the same as yesterday's closing rate for American-British. It fell by 0.0625 one hour later and continued to fall by 0.125 at closing, ending at $5.01 5625.

Securities

New York: Prices opened narrowly in the securities market this morning, with mixed ups and downs. Copper and iron stocks maintained their leading positions because public utility stocks were still being bought. Trading was generally light. The market was restrained by some profit-taking and short-covering. General security prices did not change much before noon. At noon, most security prices were slightly higher than at opening, but oil stocks remained weak. The market prices of New York stocks are listed on the left.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: The opening was quiet, but prices rose later due to new buying. Merchants had a new mindset after learning that cotton storage facilities were temporarily limited. The market still seemed to focus on weather news. October futures were 12.2, up 3 points from the close.

Chicago Wheat: The wheat and grain markets continued to receive news of declining production and rising temperatures in the Northwest, which was very favorable for the long side. The market initially rose due to good buying, but then fell below yesterday's close due to large-scale profit-taking, short-covering, and arbitrage. The price recovered later. At noon, the wheat price was 111.25, up 1/2 point, and the grain price was up 2 points. Prices continued to rise after this. The market prices of New York goods are listed on the left.

Rubber

The London silver market, rubber market, and Liverpool cotton and wheat markets were all closed today.

Commercial Inspection Group Arrives in the Philippines: Overseas Chinese Express Warm Welcome, Will Take Transportation to Java on the 6th 72

Manila Correspondence: The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group, sponsored by the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association, departed from Shanghai on the China Java Company's "Cheyne" ship on July 16. It first went to Manila in the Philippines and arrived at noon on the 23rd. It was warmly welcomed by the local overseas Chinese. The details are recorded below:

Welcome at the Wharf

The ship arrived at the port at 11:30 a.m. Consul Mo stationed in the Philippines, Chamber of Commerce Chairman Li Qingquan, Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang in the Philippines Shi Guoquan, Wu Jiqiu, and Chamber of Commerce representatives Gui Huashan, Xu Youchao, Xue Fenshi, Lin Shangchou, and more than one hundred newspaper reporters were already waiting at the pier. As soon as the ship docked, they boarded the ship to express their welcome. Subsequently, the members of the delegation disembarked, took photographs, and then took cars to the Great Eastern Hotel to rest.

Separate Visits

At 3 p.m., the head of the delegation, Gao Shiheng, the deputy head, Hu Dacheng, and the secretary, Yang Chonggao, led by Gui Huashan, visited Consul General Li stationed in the Philippines, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and the General Branch of the Party Headquarters. The leaders received them cordially and inquired about the situation in the country. At that time, Chinese and foreign newspaper reporters interviewed them one after another and competed to take photographs. They also plan to visit various authorities of the Philippine government and President Quezon within days.

Declaration Issued

After arriving in the Philippines, the delegation issued a joint declaration as a substitute for a written interview, stating that Nanyang is an area where overseas Chinese from our country gather, with vast territory, a large population, fertile land, and abundant special products. It has a long historical relationship with our country. Overseas Chinese have made great contributions to the motherland, both in spirit and material, and their enthusiasm for promoting and using domestic products is especially admired by the people of the country. In recent years, overseas Chinese have organized inspection groups to return to the motherland for sightseeing and to visit domestic product factories. They believe that domestic product industries have made significant progress in both quality and quantity. However, many overseas Chinese are unaware of this, and the domestic industrial community also believes that what is suitable for domestic sales may not be entirely suitable for foreign sales promotion. The China Industrial Foreign Trade Association, therefore, has organized the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group. Foreign trade with Europe has various relations and is not easy to start at once, so we must start with Nanyang first, because Nanyang is still a good market. Please first describe the ten major objectives of this delegation's visit to Nanyang: (1) To visit the current situation of overseas Chinese; (2) To convey the recent situation of the motherland and the achievements of active construction; (3) To announce the current situation of the domestic product community in the motherland; (4) To investigate the living conditions of overseas Chinese and the daily necessities they use, and to study improvements to suit the psychology and preferences of consumers; (5) To investigate the trends of the market and the general level of purchasing power; (6) To contact the overseas Chinese business operators to discuss methods for promoting domestic products; (7) To investigate the currency and exchange situation in various places; (8) To investigate the standards for collecting taxes and the procedures for transportation; (9) To contact overseas Chinese, introduce domestic products, and establish close contact with the domestic industrial and commercial community; (10) To visit the local highest authorities and exchange opinions. Therefore, this delegation has been here after several months of detailed preparations and has brought thousands of domestic product samples with it. Every time it arrives at a place, it will hold a public exhibition. After the exhibition period, the samples will be left in the local area to establish a more permanent domestic product display hall for the overseas Chinese to criticize and advise. We also hope to learn more from the local overseas Chinese and to conduct earnest consultations in order to communicate opinions and cooperate with each other for the purpose of mutual benefit. We do not come here with the hope of dumping products, nor do we want to use social interaction as a skill. The members of this delegation are all comrades who are actually engaged in industrial and commercial operations. We do not pursue false fame or rely on ideals, but only engage in investigation and take a pragmatic approach. We deeply hope that after this inspection, overseas Chinese in Nanyang and domestic industry and commerce will establish a close and lasting connection to revitalize our country's commercial position in the Nanyang market and prevent it from being replaced by others. This is what the members of this delegation earnestly pray for. However, as the comrades have just arrived in this area, we are unfamiliar with the place and have limited abilities. We must rely on the guidance and assistance of our overseas Chinese. Furthermore, the comrades are usually engaged in industrial and commercial operations, and we are deeply ashamed of our lack of literary skills and limited knowledge. There are many omissions and deficiencies. If we are given advice to correct our shortcomings and avoid mistakes, we will rely on your permission.

Itinerary in the Philippines

The delegation plans to stay in the Philippines for a week. The itinerary is as follows: From July 27 to August 2, a domestic product exhibition will be held. At the same time, each day, groups will be divided to hold joint discussion meetings with local trade associations (various trade associations in the Philippines). On August 3, 4, and 5, the members of the delegation will personally go to various places to conduct on-site investigations of the commercial situation and visit important local factories. On the 6th, they will take the China Java Company ship again to leave the Philippines and go to Surabaya in Java.

Zhang Fakui Arrives at Lushan to Report on the Bandit Situation in the Four Provinces; The Bandits are Still Remnants of Fang Zhimin; Most are Children in Their Teens 73

Guling Correspondence: Zhang Fakui, Commander-in-Chief for the Suppression of Bandits in the Border Areas of the Four Provinces of Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, and Anhui, arrived at Guling on the 28th and resided at No. 95. He has been reporting to Chiang Kai-shek's residence at No. 12 on the bandit situation and suppression efforts in the border areas of the four provinces and requesting instructions on everything. According to Secretary Zhu, who came to Guling with Zhang, the red bandits in the border areas of the four provinces are still the remnants of Fang Zhimin, scattered in the border areas of the four provinces. The total number of red bandits is about 1,000, with 50-60% armed with guns. Due to years of turmoil in the bandit areas, there is a severe shortage of able-bodied men. Most of the bandits are children in their teens. Supplies are extremely scarce. The bandit leader is Huang Ligui, and most of the bandits are concentrated on the Zhejiang-Fujian border, with relatively fewer on the Jiangxi-Anhui border. The bandits adopt a policy of coming out at night and scattering when the army arrives, making it extremely difficult for the army to track them down. To completely eliminate them, it is necessary to rely on local Baojia and militia groups. However, in areas affected by bandits, many of the righteous gentry, wealthy households, and intellectuals have fled, making it extremely difficult to establish sound Baojia and militia groups. In the future, the provincial governments of the four provinces must each send senior officials to be stationed in the border areas to engage in the organization of the people and the reorganization of the militia groups. This will make it easier to achieve results. Relying solely on the army will not solve the problem, etc.

Grain Prices Soar in Jilin; Flood Disasters and Harsh Government Combine to Form Divine Wrath and Popular Resentment; Japanese Puppet Officials and Merchants Ruthlessly Collude to Take Advantage of the Opportunity 75

Jilin Correspondence: Since the establishment of the puppet organization, the Northeast has been experiencing consecutive years of major disasters, and agricultural production has been greatly reduced as a result. Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been continuous rain and heavy floods. The fields along the rivers have been almost completely washed away. As a result, grain prices in Jilin have soared uncontrollably. Taking the price of soybeans as an example, the price for soybeans at the station is 2.4 yuan. Soybean cakes cost 8 jiao each, and soybean oil costs 2 jiao 8 fen. In addition, rice costs 3.5 yuan, white flour costs 3.55 yuan per bag, sorghum costs 2.2 yuan, corn costs 2.4 yuan, millet seeds cost 6 jiao, and corn flour costs 5 fen per jin. Compared to this time last year, grain prices have increased by a quarter. Compared to soybeans, the increase is more than double. White flour has also risen by about 1 yuan. In addition, there is a feeling of food shortage. Recently, a lot of Xigong rice from Dalian has been entering Jilin. Grain merchants are stockpiling, and coarse grains and miscellaneous grains are entirely transported from the Acheng County area of Harbin. Amidst the soaring grain prices in Jilin City recently, grain merchants are very active, earning three times the profit. These profiteers all have Japanese puppet officials as their background, and they divide the profits equally. However, the lives of ordinary people are filled with cries of pain and complaints. There is still no hope of grain prices falling in the near future. Towns and villages upstream of the Songhua River not only have no grain to transport downstream, but farmers are still buying and transporting grain upstream from Jilin. Recently, farmers at the junction of Huadian and Yongji counties on the Songhua River are suffering from a lack of food due to the floods of last year, which resulted in meager agricultural harvests. Under these circumstances of natural disasters and harsh government, the suffering of the people has reached its extreme.

Bandit Trouble in the Border Area of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Has Been Suppressed -- Notorious Bandit in Liangshan Also Arrested 76

Jinan Correspondence: The Cao area is located in the southwestern border area of Shandong Province, close to Hebei and Henan provinces, and has long been plagued by bandits, known as difficult to govern. In order to eradicate banditry, Han Fuju established rural agricultural schools in the western Shandong area last year, providing training to increase self-defense capabilities. Over the years, more than 24,000 people in the counties of the area have received primary and advanced training, and their strength is quite strong. As a result, bandits and petty thieves have disappeared, and the people have been able to live and work in peace. Although bandits from the neighboring provinces of Dongming, Changyuan, Lanfeng, Kaocheng, Yucheng, Dangshan, and other counties occasionally raided the area, fortunately, the people were well-trained and able to suppress them immediately. On the 11th of this month, Miao Yongqing, Hu Camel, Zhang Zouwu, and other notorious bandits from Henan Province led more than 50 bandits and suddenly raided Zhangdazhuang, 60 li from the city in the southwestern border area of Heze, kidnapping six hostages. Zhang Weibin, a graduate of the self-defense class (i.e., trained civilians), and his brother were also kidnapped at the same time. Upon hearing the news, Sun Zerang, the Second District Administrative Inspector, immediately led more than 100 soldiers and students from the rural school, traveling by car and bicycle to suppress the bandits. After arriving, the bandits fled back towards Dongming. Sun Zerang led the team in pursuit, reaching the forests of the Dasha River west of Matou Town in Dongming. The bandits were about to stop to catch their breath when they saw the government troops arriving. They immediately resisted desperately. Dai Dongsheng, the leader of the government troops' squadron, bravely went forward and fought the bandits in hand-to-hand combat, resulting in his death. Wang Dexing, a student from the rural school, also died at the same time. Subsequently, Sun Zerang led the team to arrive, surrounded and attacked them fiercely, killing countless bandits and recovering four hostages, six guns, and one horse. The bandits then broke through the encirclement and fled. The kidnapped students Zhang Weibin and his brother were still not out of danger at this time, so the pursuit continued, reaching the Hongmiao area southwest of Kaocheng. The bandits then dispersed one after another, breaking into smaller groups. While searching, Zhang Weibin, the kidnapped student, took the opportunity in a village between Lanfeng and Kaocheng to kill Miao Yongqing and the other three bandit leaders who were guarding him, obtaining two box cannons. He immediately reported to the Lanfeng County Government. After receiving the news, Sun Zerang immediately sent Captain Liu Zhijun to lead a team to retrieve him and consulted with Magistrate Yang of the county to discuss the matter of capturing the scattered bandits. The county magistrate immediately sent a team to assist, and a total of more than 30 bandits and suspects of harboring them were arrested. The bandit trouble in the border area was thus suppressed. It is now reported that Sun Zerang has returned to Heze and is gathering gentry and merchants to prepare for a memorial service for the fallen soldiers.

Liangshan is a historically famous bandit den. Although the military has severely suppressed it recently, it is still inevitable that scattered bandits gather there. Wang Qidao, a notorious bandit, nicknamed Wang Sanhanzi, also known as Lao Si, once led more than 200 bandits, fully armed with guns, and occupied Liangshan, robbing houses, kidnapping, burning, and killing, causing fear far and wide. Now, taking advantage of the rising green yarn tent, he secretly went to Yuncheng from Tianjin, using the name Fang Shouxun, and colluded with bandits from Rucheng, Dongping, Yanggu, and Shouchang counties, intending to launch a large-scale attack. An Taihe, the magistrate of Yuncheng County, led the security team and students from the self-defense class. During a meeting at the Ji Fang Zhuang, he learned that Wang Qidao was carrying several pistols and hiding at the house of Han Liu, a prostitute in Xiaoting Town. He then went there in plain clothes in the rain that night. At dawn, he arrested the bandit and obtained a pistol. It is said that the bandit was extremely fierce. When he was arrested, he even injured a member of the team with his fists.

Suzhou: Unveiling of the Bronze Statue of Xi Eming 77

The County Library Building in Suzhou Park was built in the ninth year of the Republic of China with the exclusive donation of more than 100,000 yuan from the late Shanghai pigment tycoon Xi Eming. In order to commemorate Mr. Xi, the library specially erected a bronze statue of Mr. Xi inside the building. The unveiling ceremony was held at 10 a.m. on the 1st. More than 100 guests attended. After Yang Yongshang, the chairman, reported on the details of the project, Magistrate Deng delivered a speech, followed by speeches by Zhang Yijun and others. Xi Heting, a representative of the family, delivered a thank-you speech. Then, Peng Zi, the director of the Education Bureau, unveiled the statue. After the ceremony, photographs were taken and the guests dispersed.

Through Traffic on the Entire Suzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou Road 78

Since Gui Chenqin took over the long-distance bus service on the Suzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou Highway, it has been gradually reorganized. The highway from the Pingwang station on the Suzhou-Jiaxing Road to Huzhou has also been completed, and long-distance buses began operating on the 1st. There are ten round trips every day, passing through thirteen stations along the way: Meiyan, Zhenze, Naxun East Station, Naxun West Station, Dongqian, Hucun, Jicun, Jiuguan, Chenshe, Shenshan, Balidian, Huzhou East Station, and Huzhou South Station. In order to give preferential treatment to passengers between Pingwang and Huzhou, single tickets can be used as round-trip tickets within half a month. At the same time, a 30% discount is offered on round-trip tickets for the entire Suzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou route. After the road is opened to traffic, it only takes five hours to travel from Huzhou via Suzhou (or Jiaxing) to Shanghai, which is very convenient for passengers. An official opening ceremony is scheduled for September 1.

Wuxi: Lightning Strikes and Kills a Farmer 79

Xie Yaokui, a 39-year-old resident of the tenth household in the first Jia of Lihe Township, Third District, Wuxi County, was married to the Guo family and had two sons and three daughters. His family was well-off. At about 4 p.m. yesterday, Yaokui was working in the field when the sky suddenly became overcast with dark clouds, thunder rumbled, lightning flashed, and then heavy rain poured down. With a deafening thunderclap, Yaokui was struck by lightning and died on the spot, a tragic sight. His body had purple marks on the upper part and blue marks on the lower part. His mouth and eyes were open, and there were three scorched holes on his head, which was quite bizarre. At the same time, a large branch of a tree in front of the Feng family's house near the Xuezha Bridge near Xin Town was also destroyed by lightning.

Inspecting Security Teams in Various Counties 80

Wu Delin, Deputy Commander of the Second District Security Command, in order to promote security matters in various counties, set out on the 1st with Staff Officer Xu Jiren to inspect the security teams in various counties. He will provide detailed guidance and improvements on security matters. The itinerary is scheduled for one month and he will return to Wuxi on September 5. He will compile and study the findings of the inspection.

Changzhou Unearthed a Large Quantity of Buried Gold 81

Wen Aisheng, a farmer in the Seventh District of Wuyi County, Yancheng Township, needed to dredge a shadowy area within the Mo character-numbered base in July. He led his younger brother, Xingsheng, and hired workers such as Tian Ruigen to help with the work. Suddenly, they unearthed eight gold ingots, twelve gold bars, and gold rings, silver jewelry, and silver dollars. When weighed, the gold totaled sixteen catties and six taels, estimated at over 30,000 yuan. The gold bars were inscribed with the four characters "Lu Dian Pure Gold." After obtaining the gold, Wen Aisheng gave the workers Tian Zheng 300 yuan and then went into hiding. His younger brother, Xingsheng, then filed a report with the Department of Finance, requesting the county to investigate and hand over the hidden gold, stating that it should belong to the state to avoid harm, etc. The Department of Finance has now ordered County Magistrate Hou to investigate and report back for verification.

Nantong Naval Police Deploy Defense Zones 82

Zhu Aizhou, the Commander of the Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Naval Police stationed in Tongzhou, summoned the captains and commanders of his units to discuss defense matters in the flood season. He transferred the Dongtai Jianggang team to be stationed at Pinch, and the Yancheng Huanghekou team to be stationed at Qianqiugang. The Yangtze River patrol line was extended to Jingjiang Xingang. The Junhe warship was docked at Wusong, and the Haiying warship was docked at Tianshenggang, jointly responsible for patrolling the Shengsi Islands fishing area.

Continuous Rain for Weeks Threatens Disaster 83

In Tongzhou, heavy rain has persisted for nearly ten days, causing the inland river water level to rise sharply, and low-lying fields have become swamps. Currently, all gates and culverts connecting Tongzhou to the river and sea have been opened to discharge water. Cotton seedlings have already been damaged. Given the current situation, a flood seems inevitable.

Haizhou Mahuzhuang Village Burned and Murdered by Bandits 84

Ding Zhiguo, a notorious bandit in this county, is extremely fierce. Rewards have been offered for his arrest for a long time, but he has not been captured. Recently, taking advantage of the growing green crops, he has been carrying out massacres and robberies in the southwest area. Ding and dozens of his followers went to the edge of Jinjiazhuang Village, Xingzhong Township, Fourth District, intending to enter the village and rob it. However, they were discovered by the villagers, who opened fire, preventing them from succeeding. Ding then led his men into the home of Sha Kaiyuan, a farmer in Mahuzhuang Village, west of the village, killing one of Kaiyuan's sons, wounding another, and burning Sha's house to the ground. When Lu Zipei, a neighbor, heard the alarm, he gathered over a hundred militiamen from Xingzhong and Xingxi Townships and went to encircle them. The bandits were overwhelmed and fled southwest.

Ningbo Situation in Daishan Tense Again 85

After the riots of fishermen and salt workers in Daishan, Dinghai, the local authorities took measures to appease them, and the matter subsided. Unexpectedly, because over thirty fishing boats from Fenghua returned to Daishan from the sea, careless speech caused rumors of a second riot to spread. Yu Bingxun, the new Director of the Weighing Bureau in Daishan, telegraphed Zhao, the District Commissioner, requesting him to instruct the Fenghua Fishery Association to advise the fishermen to be law-abiding and not to cause trouble. After receiving the telegram, Commissioner Zhao took the Keqiang warship from Ningbo to Daishan on the 31st to deter the situation. Furthermore, the Yanjiao Salt and Smuggling Patrol Team on Dou'ao Island, Qushan, Dinghai, discovered two to three hundred catties of uncolored fishing salt on Shen Abu's fishing boat from Fenghua on the 27th at Nantuo'ao beach. They detained the people and the boat together. At the time, many fishing boats were approaching the shore, leading to heated discussions and a noisy atmosphere. When the incident reached Chen Fengming, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, he secretly ordered the police to move the guns and important documents from the bureau to a private residence. He also immediately joined Captain Chen of the Security Team to mediate between the two sides. As a result, the patrol team released the people and the boat, confiscating the white salt, and the matter was settled. Unexpectedly, at that moment, a soldier accidentally fired a wooden-cased gun while cleaning it, wounding a soldier standing nearby in the right thigh. Upon hearing the gunshot, the residents and shops in Dou'ao on the island, thinking a great disaster had occurred, closed their doors, causing widespread panic throughout the city. Fortunately, the situation was temporary, and after the truth was clarified, order was restored.

Jiaxing Anti-Smuggling Committee Established 86

The Jiaxing County Chamber of Commerce initiated the formation of an anti-smuggling committee by merchants. After drafting regulations and preparing for a long time, the inaugural meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce on the 1st. Representatives from various trade associations participated as committee members. Gu Suming presided over the meeting, announcing the purpose of the meeting. The committee members then elected Jiang Fuqing, Lu Chujue, Chen Zhigong, Gu Suming, Jiang Weixian, Qian Boying, and Gu Fengtai as standing committee members. Jiang Fuqing was elected as the chairman of the committee, Lu Chujue as the leader of the investigation team, Jiang Weixian as the leader of the review team, and Gu Suming as the leader of the general affairs team. It was also resolved that: (1) In accordance with the regulations of the ministry, all shops, factories, and companies wholesale, purchasing, transporting, and importing foreign goods must register and obtain licenses before August 10th; (2) The inventory of foreign goods in various industries will be registered starting from August 5th.

Five Towns Prepare to Establish Disease Prevention Centers 87

The Jiaxing Urban District Public Security Bureau, in order to prevent epidemics, convened a meeting with the Joint Construction Office of the Urban District, gathering representatives from the five towns of Southeast, Beiping, Anwu, Huguang, and Zhongmu to discuss methods for preventing epidemics. It was decided that each town would establish a disease prevention center. Preparations are now underway, and they should be established soon. If any epidemics occur in the future, measures can be taken to prevent them from spreading.

Hangzhou An Engineering Office Established for the Hangzhou-Shaoxing Section 88

In order to complete the entire Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, the Ministry of Railways has appointed Zhang Haiping as the director of the Hangzhou-Shaoxing section engineering office to actively start construction, with a one-year deadline for completion. After Zhang consulted the Ministry of Railways in Beijing, he arrived in Hangzhou on the evening of the 31st. On the morning of the 1st, he crossed the river to Xiaoshan to prepare for the establishment of the engineering office and implement construction surveys. Earthwork projects are about to begin.

Cereal Association Postpones Establishment 89

The Zhejiang Provincial Cereal Storage Management Committee was originally scheduled to be established on August 1st. However, because all the committee members of the provincial government went to Shanghai to meet Huang Shaohong to discuss handover matters, they returned to Hangzhou on the evening of the 31st. The provincial government meeting was postponed to the 1st. Therefore, the Cereal Storage Committee decided to postpone its establishment until next week. The Cereal Storage Section of the Construction Department will be abolished and merged into the committee. The five major warehouses in Haining, Jinhua, Linhai, Pingyang, and Yueqing are preparing to be built in August. Due to time constraints, the agricultural product mortgage loans will be postponed until next year.

Early Rice Harvest Abundant 90

Because the rainfall was even and the weather was suitable in Zhejiang Province this summer, the early rice harvest is abundant in various counties. The new grains of the Wenzhou-Taizhou area have already been harvested. Most of the Hangzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou area in western Zhejiang is planted with mid-season rice, which can also be harvested next month. It is reported that the double-cropping rice promoted in Cixi, Zhenhai, Shaoxing, Wuyi, and other counties in eastern Zhejiang has achieved good results. The early rice harvest in the demonstration fields is 350 catties per mu, and the early rice yield in the ordinary promotion area is 300 catties per mu, an increase of more than 30% compared to last year.

Pinghu Fire Destroys Hengtai Silk Shop 91

At 6:15 p.m. on the 30th, a fire suddenly broke out at the Hengtai Silk Shop next to the Hanshui Bridge in the bustling downtown area. The fire started on the upper floor, and flames spread rapidly with thick smoke billowing. Several off-duty policemen on the Yanghe Tea House across the river spotted it and shouted for help. Immediately, gongs sounded loudly, and citizens rushed and jostled in panic. From the main street across the Hanshui Bridge to Xiaojie, the area was surrounded by water hoses. The Jinshan Dragon Brigade from the main street and the Shoushan Dragon Brigade from Xiaojie provided the most effective assistance, and the fire was extinguished after a while. The shop has been open for about twenty years. Due to its good management and timely purchase of the latest foreign goods, it has been able to stand out in the sluggish silk industry and accumulate a lot of wealth. This time, the accounting room was destroyed, and the modern clothing materials piled up upstairs and downstairs were all flooded with water. The shop had fire insurance with a Shanghai company and has telegraphed to request an investigation.

Bengbu Joyful Rainfall Amidst Severe Drought 92

Northern Anhui has suffered from a severe drought this summer, almost throughout the Huai River basin. As the flood season approached, the climate became even hotter, with the Fahrenheit temperature often around 98 degrees. The autumn crops in the fields were all wilting. Farmers eagerly awaited rain, praying to gods for rain almost every day. Unexpectedly, in the past week, the temperature suddenly changed, with dark clouds covering the sky and continuous rain, creating a pleasant and refreshing atmosphere, with cool nights like early autumn. The sky only cleared on the afternoon of the 31st. The farmers were overjoyed that the timely rain had moistened the fields and crops, raising hopes for an autumn harvest, and their faces were filled with joy.

Letter from Zou Yuou 93

To the Editors of Shen Bao:

Regarding the item in your "Overseas Correspondence" column on July 30th, which stated that the Wuxi Railway Gu Stationmaster, luggage room director, and staff members organized a smuggling ring, and that after being discovered by the railway bureau, the deputy stationmasters and relevant personnel were given demerits on the 2nd of this month; and that Zou Yuou, the former director of the Second Section stationed in Wuxi, was also involved with the smuggler Wang Xingen, and was dismissed from his position, etc., I was surprised upon reading it. After investigation, Yuou was suspended from his position by order of the Railway Police Headquarters of the Ministry of Railways on March 29th of this year. He completed the handover of his duties immediately and moved to Nanjing to live in leisure. Since he held no position, there was no dismissal to speak of. Moreover, the dismissal of the stationmasters and staff members of Wuxi stations due to the smuggling case occurred on the 2nd of this month, several months after Yuou left the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway. What your newspaper reported does not match the facts. In addition to investigating the source of the report, please correct it immediately. Thank you in advance.

Sincerely,

Zou Yuou

July

The Prospect of Turmoil in Spain 94

— Bin

The entire country of Spain is now in a fierce civil war. This turmoil is not only a domestic political struggle but also concerns the overall situation in Europe. Now, let's briefly explain the immediate causes of this turmoil.

Since the Spanish Popular Front won the election in February, the Fascists and right-wing parties have been plotting to seize power again almost every day. On the 12th of this month, when Spanish Royalist leader Sotelo was assassinated, the political situation in Spain became even more unstable. Plots of Fascist coups were uncovered almost daily. The rebellion of the Spanish Moroccan garrison and part of the domestic army launched on the 18th was a pre-planned scheme by the Royalist Party and the Fascist Party. According to their plan, they would first launch the rebellion in Morocco, then start uprisings in the country, and then converge directly on the capital. Now, the civil war is raging, and although the situation is still unclear, the fronts of both sides are very obvious: on one side is the Popular Front, supported by the vast majority of the farmers and workers who account for 80% of the Spanish population. On the other side are the rebel army, including the Royalist Party, the Fascist Party, and the big landlords and capitalists, reportedly backed by Italy and Germany. The Spanish Popular Front and the Fascists have reached a decisive battle. Spain has stepped onto an inevitable stage in the historical process.

It has been a full five years since Spain experienced an unprecedented revolution in 1931, overthrowing the thousand-year-old throne and establishing a new republican system. During these five years, the Spanish revolutionary movement has progressed through a difficult process. Peasant unrest, worker strikes and demonstrations, and the autonomy movements of oppressed ethnic groups in Catalonia, Basque, and Asturias have never stopped. This is because the Republican government cannot solve the various contradictions in social economy and ethnic issues. Although the imperial system has been overthrown, the power of the landlords is still very strong, the peasants still live the poorest inhuman life, the liberation of ethnic minorities has not been realized, and the status of labor has not been improved—it is estimated that the number of unemployed people has reached one million. Since social and ethnic contradictions are so acute, they are naturally deeply reflected in the continued political instability.

Originally, most of the past Republican governments were controlled by the right wing of the capitalist group. Under the threat of revolution, this regime accelerated to the right. Before September 1933, although the Azana cabinet, which was relatively "left," appeared for a while, it was soon overthrown. Azana was the leader of the left-wing Republican Party. Under his rule, he confiscated some aristocratic lands and slightly implemented land distribution reforms, which aroused the dissatisfaction of the nobles and big landlords. Succeeding Azana was Lerroux, representing the financial capital group, but Lerroux was soon overthrown by the united front of left-wing parties. The successor was the weak and incompetent Samper. Because of the fierce struggle between the left and right factions, the Samper cabinet was soon squeezed down. The Fascists repeatedly put Lerroux on the stage. With the active support of the right wing, Lerroux used iron-fisted policies to suppress the revolution of October 1934. Later, "Spanish Hitler" Luchs was appointed Minister of the Army, and thus the Spanish regime took the road of Fascism. By September of last year, the Fascist Party was dissatisfied with Lerroux again, reorganized the cabinet several times, and put Portela Valladares on the stage. All of them were puppets of the Fascist Party. This Valladares cabinet was overthrown in mid-February of this year due to the victory of the Popular Front in the general election.

The victory of the Spanish Popular Front was not an accident, but an inevitable result of the successful political base for the United Front of the objective situation in Spain and all strata and political parties. The more the power of the Popular Front progresses, the more intense the joint offensive of the reactionary parties will be. This is probably the inevitable "logic" of the development of social struggle. The planned large-scale rebellion provoked by the Royalist Party and the Fascist Party reflects the power of the Spanish Popular Front. In this confrontation between the rebel army and the government army, we have seen that the peasant and worker masses have organized their own militias, heroically standing up as the backbone of the government. From this, we can also see the profound mass base of the Popular Front. With the support of the broad masses, we feel that the Spanish Popular Front will not completely fail. Of course, with the joint support of the international Fascists, the right-wing rebel army in Spain may temporarily take the place of the current government. At that time, Italy and Germany will seize the opportunity to take advantage of the situation, and the international situation will change. However, given the depth of its internal contradictions and the hatred of it by the majority of the Spanish people, even if this possibility is realized, it may not be sustainable.

Reorganizing Guangdong's Finances - Borrowing 6 Million Yuan from Three Banks - Guaranteed by Guangdong's Provincial Tax Revenue - Agreed Upon by Director Song and Tang Beizhou, etc. 95

In order to reorganize Guangdong's finances, the Ministry of Finance has not only appointed Song Ziliang as the Special Commissioner for Guangdong's Finances and the Director of Finance, but also appointed Directors Zou Lin and Zhou Shouliang, Deputy Director of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank; Li Tisheng, Deputy Director of the National Treasury Bureau; Bei Songsun, Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China; and Tang Shoumin, General Manager of the Bank of Communications to assist in Guangzhou, establish a Guangzhou branch of the Central Bank, and reform the silver dollar system. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency learned from banking circles yesterday that Chen Jitang, Chen Weizhou, Qu Fangpu, and others of Guangdong Province took away a large amount of silver reserves and tax revenues when they fled, making reorganization difficult. Now, the Guangdong government is borrowing 6 million yuan in national currency from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications for the purpose of reorganizing Guangdong's finances. The loan is guaranteed by Guangdong's provincial tax revenue. Quality Inspection of Exported Raw Silk Began Yesterday 97

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce began conducting quality inspections of raw silk yesterday, allowing grade inspections to wait until next year. All white filature silk exported from Shanghai must have a certificate issued by the bureau in order to be declared for export. Various foreign firms and silk manufacturers are applying to the bureau for quality inspections in accordance with the regulations. The bureau issues inspection certificates, noting the uniformity score, average denier, minimum uniformity score, denier deviation, cleanliness score, denier difference, cleanliness score, tensile strength in centimeters, European style cutting, elongation, cohesiveness, etc. The technicians and trainees who were recruited and trained are already working. Since the implementation, various export firms and silk manufacturers have said it is convenient. As for the grade inspection, it is scheduled to be implemented on February 1st next year.

Three Branch Roads of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Highway Completed - Opening to Traffic in Succession - Transportation Becoming More Convenient 98

Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou, Wuxi-Shanghai, and Suzhou-Jiaxing highways in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, passenger and freight transportation has become more convenient. Recently, the two provinces have been actively constructing branch roads to develop inland transportation. There are three branch roads that have been opened to traffic: (1) The section of the highway between Kunshan and Taicang was completed in February of this year and opened to traffic immediately. It was then extended to Liuhe. The road surface project was also completed in June. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction has sent personnel to conduct acceptance inspections. The roadside stations have also been surveyed and constructed. The Suzhou-Kunshan-Taicang Highway Office is planning to operate passenger buses and is scheduled to open to traffic on the 10th of this month. (2) The Hangzhou-Jiaxing highway has been completed and opened to traffic on the 1st of this month, connecting with the Suzhou-Jiaxing and Shanghai-Hangzhou highways. The entire journey can be reached in five hours. Buses run twice a day. A supplementary traffic opening ceremony is scheduled for the 1st of next month. (3) The construction of the Huzhou-Jiaxing highway has been completed. A trial run was conducted on the 15th of last month. Because a part of the road surface was not strong enough, it was repaired and opened to traffic on the 1st of this month. The road passes through Nanxun and Zhenze to Pingwang, connecting with the Suzhou-Jiaxing highway. All three roads are connected to the railway.

Nanjing Municipal Government Loan to be Allocated Immediately - Borrowed from the Central Trust Bureau for Five Years at 8% Weekly Interest 100

According to the Central News Agency, the Nanjing Municipal Government is borrowing 1.7 million yuan in national currency from the Central Trust Bureau to expand the capital's water supply and drainage projects. The board of directors has approved it and drafted a contract, which the Nanjing Branch has sent to the Municipal Government for review. Yesterday morning, Deputy Director Zhang of the bureau told reporters that as soon as they receive a telephone notification from the Nanjing Municipal Government, they can sign the contract and allocate the funds. According to the contract, the loan is secured by all the assets of the capital's water plant and 600,000 yuan of the city's special construction bonds. The revenue of the plant and the funds allocated from the Gengkuan for the city's drainage construction will be used to repay the principal and interest on a monthly basis. The loan term is five years, starting from July of the second year, which is the 36th year of the Republic of China, and the principal and interest will be repaid once a month. The interest rate is 8% per week.

Wheat Exported to Japan - 18,000 Tons Have Been Shipped - Purchased by Mitsui, Mitsubishi, and Yoshida 101

According to the Japanese newspaper Nichinichi Shimbun, Japan decided not to buy Australian wheat in retaliation for Australia's tariffs, causing various problems in the economic world. The impact on Shanghai is wheat. Japanese merchants who decided not to buy Australian wheat and instead purchased Chinese wheat have centered on Shanghai. A large amount of wheat from the wheat-producing areas in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River has been purchased by Japanese merchants. In July, the Shanghai branch of Nippon Yusen Kaisha transported 18,000 tons to Japan (mostly shipped to Yokohama), so every ship was fully loaded. The buyers of these wheats are Mitsui, Mitsubishi, Yoshida, etc. They are still continuing to purchase.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Explains Doubts Regarding Stamp Duty 106

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday replied to a letter from the Liangyou Factory, stating, "In response to your letter of the 31st of this month regarding various points concerning the method of affixing stamp tax, we have understood the details. Our response is as follows: (1) If the stamp is a two-part form, the part given to the customer should be stamped, and the part kept in the store for verification is, according to Article 3 of the Implementing Regulations of the Stamp Tax Law, a copy that is completely identical in content to the original, only for verification purposes and not for use. Based on Article 3, Section 7 of the Stamp Tax Law, it is not necessary to affix a stamp. (2) If both the remittance slip to the bank and the receipt given to the other party are fully stamped, then according to Article 12 of the Implementing Regulations of the Stamp Tax Law, which states that "various bills that should be subject to stamp tax according to the Stamp Tax Law, if bound into booklets, should be stamped for each item before use or delivery," it is not necessary to affix stamps to the booklets themselves. (3) The handbooks used by workers to receive wages from the factory, according to the regulations in Item 4 of the tax-exempt column of the Stamp Tax Rate Table, do not need to be stamped. (4) The price list is not specified in the Stamp Tax Rate Table. Its effect, before a transaction is completed, is to attract customers and is different in nature from invoices and bills, so it does not need to be stamped. (5) Although temporary receipts are not specified in the tax-exempt column of Item 2 of the tax rate table, by analogy with temporary subscription receipts and temporary vouchers, it seems that they may be exempt from stamping. The Chamber has submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for instructions, but has not yet received a reply."

Municipal Federation of Trade Unions Petitions Ministry of Industry to Strive for Sovereignty in Factory Inspections. Tragic Accidents in Factories in the Concession are Commonplace. If Improvements Are Not Made Soon, Where Will the Disasters End? 108

According to Dagong News Agency, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions submitted a document to the Ministry of Industry stating, "The issue of factory inspections in the Shanghai International Settlement has been under negotiation for five years. During this time, the municipal government has repeatedly negotiated with the concession authorities. Only in June of this year did the Municipal Council and the municipal government jointly draft an agreement on factory inspections in the International Settlement. The content of the agreement is barely satisfactory, and we were looking forward to its implementation to improve the lives of hundreds of thousands of workers. However, according to recent reports, after the agreement was passed by the Municipal Council's board of directors, the Consular Body believed that the agreement could lead to the abolition of part of the extraterritorial privileges granted by the treaties of countries with consular jurisdiction and demanded amendments. They believe that the agreement should only be implemented in Chinese factories 'and factories of countries without consular jurisdiction' in the concession. As for the handling of inspection matters in factories of countries with consular jurisdiction, it is a right granted by the Yangjingbang Regulations and should be handled by the Municipal Council through the issuance of licenses. According to the Yangjingbang Regulations mentioned by the Consular Body, the right to factory inspection was obtained through the issuance of licenses, but the Chinese people at the time opposed it, and the government did not recognize it. Even the Municipal Council itself found the licensing method too difficult to implement. Therefore, the grounds cited by the Consular Body are inappropriate. Furthermore, the implementation of factory inspections not only benefits workers but also reduces accidental losses for factories and ensures the safety of the entire factory. At the same time, it is also of great importance to public health and social welfare. This is a matter of the entire society and humanitarianism and should not be discussed from a diplomatic or political point of view. Recalling the boiler explosions in the Zhengtai and Taiyi factories last year, which killed and injured more than a hundred male and female workers, such tragic accidents are common in factories in the concession. If factory inspections are not implemented soon, the disasters in the future are unimaginable. In view of this, the Federation has repeatedly decided to petition your ministry to expedite negotiations on the matter of factory inspections in concession factories and to promote its early implementation. We now restate the reasons and petition your ministry to continue negotiations based on reason and strive to achieve the goal. The Federation, on behalf of more than 800,000 workers in the city, is willing to be the backing, and we present this petition urgently and with great anticipation. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Minister of Industry, Shanghai General Labor Union, by acting Chairman Zhou Xuexiang, Standing Committee Members Ye Xianggao, Nan Mengnan, Zhang Kechang, Shao Xubai, and Long Peiyun."

In 1928, the government resolved to recover customs autonomy. At that time, I assisted former Foreign Minister Wang (Zhengting) in persistently striving for this goal with ambassadors from various countries, and finally achieved the goal of customs autonomy. In the future, I will continue the spirit of past efforts and work diligently under the instructions of Minister Kong. As for the staff in the office, except for a few people who will go to Guangdong with former Superintendent Tang, there will be no major changes. I hope that people from all walks of life will often give guidance to correct my shortcomings."

Sichuan Sojourners Association in Shanghai Cables Request to Punish Smuggling Sichuan Merchants, Chongqing Customs Detains 500-600 Bags 112

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Sichuan Sojourners Association in Shanghai recently cabled a request to the government to stop Sichuan merchants from transporting smuggled goods and to punish the treacherous merchants. The telegram is as follows: (Titles Omitted) "We recently received a letter from the Sichuan Merchants Public Welfare Association, stating that eleven member firms reported that the Chongqing Customs had detained more than 600 bags of smuggled goods shipped from North China to Sichuan, estimated to be worth 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. The consignees of these postal bags are Chengdu Transportation Company, Jin Longtai, Zhenxing Company, Jin Yichang, Jin Yisheng, Yipuheng, Baoyuanlong, Tongtaichang, and other firms. We believe that smuggling in North China affects national tax revenue and the livelihood of legitimate merchants nationwide, harms the country, and poisons the people of Sichuan. Therefore, we request the Public Welfare Association to forward this report to the Chongqing Superintendent's Office and various government agencies, requesting them to thoroughly detain the smuggled goods in accordance with the anti-smuggling laws specially issued by the central government, confiscate and auction them, and punish the treacherous merchants to serve as a warning to others.' Based on this, we find that amidst the illegal establishment of a consulate in Chengdu by Japan, shameless treacherous merchants are transporting large quantities of smuggled goods, which has a profound and significant impact on our national economy. To protect the country and the nation and to care for the interests of our hometown, we specially cable your Yuanbu to stop smuggling, legally detain the goods, and severely punish the treacherous merchants to serve as a warning to others and to maintain the rule of law." Sichuan Sojourners Association in Shanghai, bowed, East.

Savings Deposits in the Four Banks Savings Society Exceed 80 Million Yuan 114

More Than Any Other Bank in China

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Ji業 Bank, China and South Bank, Jincheng Bank, and Continental Bank jointly established the Four Banks Savings Society in the spring of 1923, with Wu Dingchang as the director and Qian Xinzhi as the deputy director. They specialize in receiving various savings deposits, including fixed-term, long-term, installment, and demand deposits. All operations strictly comply with the regulations of savings banks, and the management is primarily stable, which has gained the trust of the people. The total amount of savings deposits has increased from more than 1.4 million yuan to 80 to 90 million yuan. The interest and dividends earned by depositors are as high as 1.17% per week and no lower than 0.87%. At the end of June this year, the settlement period for the first half of the year ended, and the savings deposits amounted to 84,425,867.48 yuan, which is more than the savings deposits of any other bank savings society or trust company in China. However, the weekly interest and dividends for the first half of this year were 0.87%.

Municipal Police Bureau Reforms Household Registration System 116

According to Shenshi News Agency, since Director Cai of the Municipal Police Bureau took office on an installment payment plan, he believes that household registration can assist in maintaining public security. However, the original household registration system cannot meet the needs of the times. He is determined to reform it and has ordered his subordinates to formulate plans and budget estimates, which have been submitted to the municipal government for approval and are being implemented step by step. In addition to the city-wide household registration review and the replacement of household registration cards, which have been carried out effectively, the existing household registration patrol officers and household registration police officers in the various sub-bureaus have recently been changed to household registration officers and household registration students in accordance with the Shanghai Household Registration Investigation Regulations. It is understood that this reform has been implemented in July of this year. The purpose is to simplify the work of the household registration personnel in each sub-bureau and strengthen their work force to achieve greater effectiveness. At the same time, an assessment method has been formulated, and all personnel in each sub-bureau will be assessed once a year, with promotions and demotions to provide encouragement.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Implements Treasury Collection Method Yesterday 117

State-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company issued a public notice yesterday to implement the treasury collection method. The notice stated, "The treasury collection method of this bureau will be implemented from August 1. In the future, all freight and other collections will be issued with receipts. In addition to the signature of the receiving officer and the seal of the treasury director, the official seal of the bureau will also be affixed to ensure solemnity. For freight paid on delivery, the treasury will affix the 'China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Bill of Lading Emblem' stamp on the bill of lading after receiving the payment and will also issue a receipt and a notification slip. The payer will then hand the notification slip to the import counter of the business department for verification, and the 'Import Declaration' stamp will be affixed to the bill of lading. Only with these two stamps can the goods be picked up. This is hereby announced."

Hongxing Sock Factory Dismisses Workers, Mediation Yesterday Unsuccessful 120

Since the labor dispute occurred in the Hongxing Sock Factory on Caishi Road in the French Concession, the stalemate has lasted for a month. After persuasion from party and government organs, the workers were ordered to return to work first, and the dispute would be mediated according to the law. The workers complied with the authorities' instructions and returned to work on the 26th of last month. In order to resolve the labor dispute, the Municipal Party Department specially summoned both labor and management representatives to mediate the matter the day before yesterday. Li Yaoting, the representative of the management, and Zhang Zhuyun, Shi Xiuying, and Deng Yixin, the representatives of the labor, were present. Chairman Li Weixiong of the Municipal Party Department first inquired about the opinions of both parties. The management stated that they could not reinstate the dismissed workers Shi Xiuying and others and would give them severance pay in addition to deducting overdrafts: 80 yuan to Deng Yixin, 60 yuan to Shi Xiuying, and 40 yuan to the other six workers. However, the labor side believed that the dismissal of the workers was unjustified and did not want to be dismissed, so the mediation was unsuccessful. The labor side will submit another report to the authorities, requesting the factory to allow them to return to work in order to avoid another labor dispute.

Shanghai District Court Implements Notarization System 122

Public Notice Effective August 1

The Ministry of Judicial Administration recently launched a notarization system modeled after the precedents of European and American countries. Starting from August 1, Shanghai courts will be the first to pilot the system. After the Shanghai District Court of Nanshi received the order from the High Court, it specially established a notarization office in the real estate registration office and appointed a clerk to handle the matter. Yesterday, President Lu Yimei also issued a public notice stating, "Public Notice: According to Jiangsu High Court Instruction No. 523, 'In accordance with the telegram from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, it is planned to set August 1 of this year as the date for the Shanghai Special District Court and the Shanghai District Court to implement notarization, in order to ensure uniformity. In addition to separate orders, the Shanghai District Court is ordered to actively prepare and implement as scheduled, and report back.' We have prepared in accordance with this and have established a notarization office within the court, which will begin operations on August 1 of this year. In addition to reporting and separate letters, we hereby affix a copy of 'Brief Explanation of the Notarization System' and issue a public notice in advance. In the future, for legal acts such as concluding contracts or other facts concerning the creation, loss, transfer, or modification of private rights, there is no need to apply to the court for registration. You should submit a written or verbal request to the notarization office of this court to create a notarization or authenticate a private document, so that it can be protected by the power of notarization and avoid all future disputes. This matter concerns the implementation of a new system and the protection of private rights. People within the jurisdiction should be aware of this. This public notice is specially issued."

Sri Lanka Study Group Feels Nostalgic for Homeland in Times of Trouble 123

Buddhist Association Receives Report from the Group

The five members of the Sri Lanka Study Group organized by the Chinese Buddhist Association, including Ping Song, Wei Zhi, Fa Zhou, Wei Huan, and Xiu Lu, set sail from Shanghai on May 6 of this year and arrived in Sri Lanka on June 26. Their first report was published in the newspapers. The Chinese Buddhist Association received the group's second report yesterday. Excerpts are as follows: "After arriving here, we visited the major ancient temples in Colombo, the Temple of the Tooth in the ancient palace of Kandy, and the stone cave where the Pali Tipitaka was compiled, located 50 miles from Kandy. The compilation time was approximately 80 years before the Western calendar. The architecture of the Sri Lankan Buddhist temples consists of several monk's dormitories, a Buddha hall, a stupa, and a bodhi tree, which is revered by the people in the same way as the Buddha's relics. There are few monks, but they all follow the sutras. What we have learned from the sutras, vinaya, and biographies in China is almost all seen in daily practice here. Everything, everything, is as if the Buddha's world is not far away. We are now living in the deep mountains at 3932 feet, practicing sutra rituals and living here for two months. The climate here is cool, like Guling in China. It is currently the rainy season here. Two months later, we will return to Colombo to receive the precepts of a bhikkhu. After receiving the precepts of a bhikkhu, we will go to the Madena beach, about 100 miles from Colombo, to practice the Buddhist practice of living in seclusion. A week later, we will visit the Andala Zha Bu Tuo ancient temple, (transliteration), the second oldest temple in Sri Lanka, the site of the world's oldest bodhi tree. Reading the English newspapers, we learned that our homeland is in trouble again. We regret that we cannot understand the hard work of our compatriots in defending the country. If you could kindly send us a copy of the Shanghai newspaper, we would be most grateful."

It was resolved to hold it on the 15th of this month. A regular large-scale petition was resolved to be decided at the founding meeting. National Goods Raincoat Fabric is Adopted by the Ministry of Industry 127

The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association received notice No. 16513 of the Ministry of Industry, stating, "The Secretariat of the Executive Yuan approved letter No. 5009 on the 6th of this month, stating, 'Premier instructed the Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association on June 26, 25th year, to submit three points to clarify the difference between national goods raincoat fabric and paint cloth and non-national goods. The Ministry of Finance and Industry shall handle the case of requesting all agencies to thoroughly investigate merchants who conceal purchasing personnel and pretend to use foreign goods as national goods to hinder the development of national goods, order them to adopt national goods products uniformly, and increase import tariffs on foreign raincoat fabrics, etc., in order to promote the case and issue instructions to the Ministry of Finance and Industry.' Attached is a copy of the original letter and attached samples of the base cloth and a package of photos to the ministry. In addition to requesting the increase of foreign goods, the Ministry of Finance will consult with the provincial and municipal authorities, instructing them to know and adopt national goods rain paint cloth as much as possible, and notify the association to know it. I hereby notify you. Minister Wu Dingchang.

Xu Wancheng is Sent to New Puyutang Due to Illness 128

Detained for two months, suffering from rotten feet

Xu Wancheng, the owner and editor of Longmen Bookstore on Zhonghua Road, Bainong Lane, Dananmen, was prosecuted by Zhao, a prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court, for allegedly interfering with his reputation. Xu Wancheng immediately stated that the victim was a judge of the original court, fearing bias, and applied for transfer of jurisdiction. With the approval of the Jiangsu High Court, the Wuxian District Court was designated to accept the case. The acceptance office of the transfer has not yet been welcomed and is still detained in the Shanghai Court Detention Center. However, Xu has been detained until now, and it has been two months. He is suffering from illness and his feet are rotten, making it impossible for him to move. Therefore, he submitted a statement to the court requesting to be sent to the hospital for treatment. Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association Uses X-Ray Fluoroscopy 129

Lung screening for elementary school teachers in the city

The Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association recognizes that tuberculosis is rampant and deeply harmful to young people. In particular, the spread of pulmonary tuberculosis in primary schools is even more alarming. It is found that the infection of children's pulmonary tuberculosis is due to low contact with adults suffering from lung disease. Therefore, the health of primary school teachers is closely related to students. In order to prevent it, the association will first conduct X-ray lung examinations for primary school teachers in this city. The Municipal Education Bureau issued a notice to primary schools in the city a few days ago, instructing teachers to take turns to go to the association's first clinic for examination during the autumn semester. The examination period will last from September 1 to the end of October. It is heard that after receiving the order, the principals of various primary schools have notified teachers and staff to go for examination at that time. This is indeed an important work in the anti-tuberculosis sound and a gospel for building public health.

Special Margin for Cotton Yarn Cancelled 132

The Yarn Market Exchange issued a notice yesterday

The Shanghai Chinese Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange previously charged a special cash deposit of [unclear] yuan per package for cotton transactions on July 3 due to soaring yarn and flower prices, and a special deposit of eight yuan per package for cotton yarn starting from July 11. Now that the market price has stabilized, the exchange issued Notice No. 1934 yesterday, canceling it immediately. The original text reads, "From August 1, the special cash deposit of three yuan for cotton in the October, November, and December contracts and the special cash deposit of eight yuan for cotton yarn in the September, October, November, and December contracts will be canceled. All special deposits for the above-mentioned cotton and yarn contracts that have been canceled will be returned on August 3. In addition to notifying the brokers' association, this is hereby announced."

The Second Old-Age Home in Baoan Opened Yesterday 134

The Charity Hospital on North Chengdu Road in the Public Concession has been preparing for several months since it was reorganized into the Second Old-Age Home. It is now ready. The opening ceremony was held at 2 p.m. yesterday. Representatives from the Shanghai Charity Group, Qin Yanqiao, Huang Xingjie, Kang Zhuming, representatives from the Women's Correctional Institution, Ye [unclear], representatives from the First Old-Age Home, Zheng Xiangen, representatives from the Shanghai Vagrant Training Institute, Cao Boxun, and the principal of Hean Elementary School, Xu Peixing, and many others were present. After performing the ceremony, Qin Yanqiao, the chairman, reported on the opening situation, followed by Wu Fansun, the organizer, reporting on the preparations, followed by Xu Peixing, a guest, giving a speech, followed by Qin Yanqiao and Huang Xingjie giving instructions to the elderly. Tea and snacks were served and the meeting adjourned. It is also learned that the institution is tentatively scheduled to accommodate 40 elderly people, all of whom must be over 60 years old. Women are not accepted. Thirteen people have been admitted yesterday. After entering the institution, each person is issued a set of blue cloth short shirt, pants, shoes, and socks, a pillow, mat, and blue cloth quilt, and a three-foot small iron bed. The air in the bedroom is fresh and the sunlight is sufficient, which is very hygienic. Other facilities such as dining room, washroom, bathroom, treatment room, lecture hall, and aftercare room (i.e., mortuary) are all available. Three meals are provided every three days, one porridge and two rice, i.e., porridge for breakfast and dry rice for lunch and dinner, but all vegetarian. Meat is served four times a month, it is said.

The Hotel Industry Union Discussed Yesterday Abolishing Extra Gratuities 138

The Shanghai Hotel Industry Union convened a discussion meeting on implementing the New Life Movement and abolishing the issue of extra gratuities at the union's auditorium at No. 1 Zhian Lane, Luxiang Garden Road, Nine Mu Land, at 9 a.m. yesterday. More than 100 representatives from the Shanghai New Life Movement and the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions attended. Zhu Tiwu was appointed as chairman to lead the ceremony. The chairman then read out the New Life General Assembly's principles for abolishing extra gratuities and implementing them, and explained in detail the significance of convening this discussion meeting and the advantages and disadvantages of members implementing the New Life. Then, Fang Rusheng, a representative of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, gave a speech and instructed on the steps to be taken, and the discussion began. Three methods were decided on at the time: the salary after abolishing extra gratuities; the distribution of gratuities; and the issue of pledge money. All three items have detailed and appropriate methods, which will be submitted by the association for discussion at the next Shanghai New Life Movement meeting. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock.

Forcing Re-Entry into the Bandit Gang 139

Jin A'er is determined not to obey

Jin A'er, 22 years old, from Haimen, lives at No. 36 Jinkang Lane, North Station. He was previously unemployed and made friends with Zhu A'gen (31 years old, from Kunshan), Li Chongwen (40 years old, from Changshu), and Wang Zhang and others. Who knew that Zhu, Li, Wang, Zhang, etc. specialized in robbing men and women of silver dollars, gold jewelry, and other properties, and taught the art to Jin, ordering him to join the gang and rob. Soon after, they lost their way, were captured by detectives, and sentenced to one year in prison. After being released from prison, Jin's mother taught him bitterly, and A'er made up his mind not to engage in this robbery career again, willing to endure hardship and sell fruits to support his mother. After two years of leisure, he accidentally met Zhu and Li on the road this week. They forced him to re-enter the bandit gang. Jin firmly refused and was taken to a small inn in Mantingfang, where Jin was tied up and privately executed by hanging. Later, Jin took the opportunity to bite off the rope and escaped. However, at 1:10 p.m. yesterday, Jin met the bandit gang of Zhu, Li, etc. again on Dajing Road, and they started beating him. Jin desperately tried to escape and was robbed of his small teapot, etc. by Zhu, Li, etc., causing Jin to be bruised and bleeding. He shouted for help. With the help of police officer Zhao Zhenhua, the two thieves, Zhu and Li, were detained at the Laozhamen Police Station. After questioning, it was found that the case was related to twisting and suing, ordering them to join the bandit gang and injuring them for refusing. They were sentenced to be handed over to the bureau for handling according to law.

Thunder Strikes Shed, Calamity Extends to Plowing Cattle, Causing Death 141

On the west side of the Meilong Town Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, Zhoujiazhai, Songyi, the 13-year-old eldest son of farmer Ji Tugeng, Afa, was using plowing cattle to draw water to irrigate rice in the Maojia Port shed behind his house at 4:20 p.m. yesterday. Suddenly, there was a thunderclap and lightning struck from the top of the shed. The plowing cattle were electrocuted and died instantly. The straw covering the shed was also scorched into a hole, while Afa was safe and sound, but suffered a great fright. Lü Fangzheng Falsely Claims to be from Hubei Provincial Bank, Forges Subsidiary Coin Tickets, Claims that Huaxin Company is Not Large, 50,000 Yuan Confiscated by Xiaguan Customs, Liu Peiqing Asks Lawyer to Report to Police Station 145

Lü Fangzheng, a native of Hubei, used to be a doctor. Recently, he was suspected of forging a letter of appointment from the Hubei Provincial Bank and privately printing 50,000 yuan worth of subsidiary coins of 5 jiao, 2 jiao, and 1 jiao of the bank. Someone reported it to the Xinzha Police Station, which specially dispatched Chinese detective Ma Derong and Yang Yunfeng to arrest Lü Fangzheng and take him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Court No. 8 of the First Special District Court and requested to be detained. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, stated that at noon yesterday, Yu Jizhang, a representative sent by Liu Peiqing, the owner of Huadong Engraving Company at No. 25 Maoyi Lane, No. 153 Meibaige Road, and the lawyer Li Mo reported to the police station, saying that in March of this year, the defendant Lü Fangzheng suddenly came and said that he had opened the Huaxin Printing Company in Hankou, Hubei. In January of this year, he was entrusted by Jia Shiyi, the manager of the Hubei Provincial Bank, to print 1.5 million subsidiary coins of 1 jiao, 5 jiao, and 2 jiao. However, because the Huaxin Company was not large and engraving was not its strong point, it was specially entrusted to Liu Peiqing to handle it on his behalf, clarifying that the printing fee was more than 100,000 yuan, and the profits would be split equally in the future. Because Liu had not obtained a certificate from the bank, he did not dare to agree rashly. Later, the defendant presented a letter of entrustment from the Hubei Provincial Bank as proof, and Liu believed it to be true. On March 20 of this year, Liu signed a contract with the defendant and started working. He had paid more than 3,000 yuan for raw materials and labor costs. On July 19, he first printed 50,000 yuan worth of tickets and handed them to the defendant to take to Hubei for delivery. The defendant then embarked on the Ruiyang ship and passed through Xiaguan, Nanjing. During the inspection by Jianghai Customs, the defendant became suspicious and went ashore to abscond. The forged 50,000 yuan worth of coins was confiscated. Later, the defendant sent a letter from Jiujiang to Liu Peiqing, stating the process of the coins being copied. Liu was very suspicious after reading it. Since the subsidiary coins were entrusted by the Hubei Provincial Bank, why would they be copied by the Customs? There must be a hidden reason. He immediately telegraphed Jia Shiyi in Hubei according to the address stated by the defendant on weekdays to inquire about the place, but there was no such person as Jia Shiyi in that place (it was found that Jia was the director of the Hubei Finance Office and the manager of the Hubei Provincial Bank, not a resident of that place), so the original telegram was returned, which was obviously forged. He investigated the whereabouts of the defendant everywhere. Yesterday, the defendant went to Liu Peiqing's place to ask for the return of the copper and zinc plates, so he immediately reported to the police station and arrested the defendant. Two engraved plates, eight printing plates, and a contract were copied. According to the defendant's statement at the police station, this matter was cooperated with Yang Xianqing, who is at large, in Hankou, etc. According to Liu Peiqing's complaint about the above situation, when asked, Lü Fangzheng confessed to forging the subsidiary coins, but he had made it clear to Liu Peiqing in advance that they would cooperate, etc. Judge Tan Xinzhen verified the confession and said that it was necessary to investigate the case with Nanjing Customs, so he ordered Lü Fangzheng to be detained for seven days for further interrogation. The copper and zinc plates, etc. will be stored in the warehouse first.
