Law Enforcement Detective "Fool" in the French Concession: Falsely Accusing a Good Woman of Being a Prostitute, Kicking Her Causing a Miscarriage, Illegally Inflicting Private Torture Resulting in Serious Danger to the Mother 147

Citizens' Association of the Second Special District Sends Letter to French Consul-General

The Kuomin News Agency reports that the Citizens' Association of the Second Special District of this city sent a letter yesterday to the French Consul-General in Shanghai, stating that a citizen, Wang Aidi, had a verbal dispute with someone. She was then taken to the police station by a detective from the French Concession. Another detective, nicknamed "Fool," falsely accused her of being a prostitute and inflicted private torture on her by punching and kicking her, which caused injury to her six-month pregnancy. The next day, she suffered severe abdominal pain, and the police station released her to go home. On the evening of the ninth, at 12:00 midnight, she vomited blood. At about 1:00 AM, she miscarried. Because the fetus had been injured, it died immediately after birth. The woman's condition is also very dangerous. The original letter from the Second Special District Citizens' Association to the French Consul-General and the French Police Commissioner is as follows: "To whom it may concern, according to a letter from the Third District Branch of our association, and a letter from citizen Zhu Zhou, it is stated that her niece, Wang Aidi, was standing idly at the entrance of an alley on the evening of the seventh of this month when she had a minor verbal dispute with a stranger. Two detectives, without investigating the circumstances, took the niece to the MacLellan Road police station, and then transferred her to the Lujiiawan police station. There, a French detective nicknamed 'Fool' falsely accused her of being a prostitute and inflicted private torture on her by kicking and punching her, causing damage to her six-month pregnancy. The next day, due to severe abdominal pain, the police station released her to go home at 4:00 PM. On the evening of the ninth, at 12:00 midnight, she vomited blood. At about 1:00 AM, she gave birth prematurely. Because the fetus had been seriously injured, the baby died immediately after birth. The niece's condition is deteriorating daily and is in imminent danger. We have always admired your association's role in safeguarding citizens' rights, and we dare to state the facts. We respectfully request that you uphold justice, negotiate, and seek redress." After sending personnel to investigate, the facts were confirmed. The French detective's abuse of power, infliction of private torture, and disregard for human life are clearly violations of criminal law. We request that your association forward a serious protest to the French authorities to punish the perpetrator in order to uphold human rights, etc. Based on this information, it has been found that, recently, police detectives have abused their power and neglected their duties frequently. The detective falsely accused a good woman of being a prostitute, inflicted private torture and beatings, which caused injury and miscarriage to a six-month pregnancy. This is extremely illegal. Based on the aforementioned facts, we hereby request that Your Excellency the Consul-General (Commissioner) thoroughly investigate and severely punish the perpetrator, and at the same time, instruct subordinates to ensure that similar incidents do not occur again, in order to maintain public order and safety for citizens. We hope that you will investigate and handle this matter accordingly, and we look forward to your reply. This letter is addressed to the French Consul-General in Shanghai, Mr. Bados, (Commissioner Fabre)."

Lü Zongying Uses Promissory Notes to Defraud Airline Ticket Sales; Hongtai Bank Goes Bankrupt; Detective Tracks Down and Arrests Him 148

Lü Zongying from Zhenjiang, 36 years old, residing at 57 Xin Yong'an Street in the French Concession, operated the Hongtai Bank on Avenue Edward VII. In April of this year, using the name of the Detai Cigarette Paper Store at 43 Yong'an Street, he obtained 200 tickets for the 22nd issue of the airline lottery from the Da Yun Company on Avenue Edward VII. In early May, he again obtained 200 airline tickets from the company in his own name and provided a promissory note for 4,850 yuan dated May 8 from Hongtai Bank. When Da Yun Company attempted to cash the note at the bank when it matured, the Hongtai Bank had already gone bankrupt and declared liquidation, and Lü had disappeared without a trace. Da Yun Company then reported the matter to the French police and requested an investigation. Only the other day, detective Tao Desheng and other detectives from the French police encountered Lü Zongying in the International Settlement. After careful observation, they followed him to the intersection of Tianzhu Tang Street on Avenue Edward VII and arrested him, taking him to the police station. Yesterday, together with the complainant, Da Yun Company representative Li Mingzhen, Lü was sent to the Second Special District Court for questioning. Judge Sun Peng, serving in the Eighth Criminal Court, presided over the trial. The Police Department's lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, presented the case, requesting a postponement for further investigation and then requesting a trial. The court briefly questioned the defendant and ordered a postponement until August 8 for further hearing. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Chen Huizhang Case Support Association: Hosts Guests From All Walks of Life Today; Rickshaw Pullers Issue Declaration of Support 149

The Chen Huizhang Case Support Association, formed after the tragic killing of Chen Huizhang by a British sailor, will hold a reception for guests from all walks of life at the Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association at Tan Jiaqiao on Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, at 2:00 PM today. The telegram from the association and the declaration of all rickshaw pullers are recorded below: (1) Telegram (details omitted) It is noted that rickshaw puller Chen Huizhang was injured and killed by a British sailor. The authorities in the concession have not indicated how the perpetrators will be punished, which is deeply alarming. This is not only a matter of vital interest to our fellow Jianghuai residents in Shanghai, but also closely related to the integrity of the nation. All Chinese people should speak out in unison and strive together to protect our national rights and respect our people's lives. Filled with righteous indignation, how can we remain silent? We have convened an emergency meeting and resolved to establish the Chen Huizhang Case Support Association, the purpose of which is to seek punishment for the perpetrators and ensure that similar incidents do not happen again. In addition to submitting this to the Party and government organs for record and urging serious negotiations, we are sending this telegram to express our concern for national rights and human lives. We hope you will support us and jointly send a telegram to the central government departments urging them to punish the perpetrators and uphold justice and national dignity. It would be fortunate for the nation and the people. The Chen Huizhang Case Support Association respectfully bows. (2) Yesterday, all rickshaw pullers in the city issued a declaration of support, stating: We rickshaw pullers rely on our physical strength to transport passengers and earn a meager income to make a living. It is truly miserable. Seeking compensation for pulling the rickshaw is a legitimate right. Unexpectedly, recently, a British sailor, claiming to be from a civilized nation, refused to pay the fare after riding in a rickshaw. Rickshaw puller Chen Huizhang, seeing that the fare was being denied, tried to retrieve it, but was instead beaten to death by the sailor. The circumstances are shocking. Although the occupation of rickshaw puller is humble, we are also part of the citizens of the Republic of China. The sailor dared to disregard discipline, act lawlessly, disregard sovereignty, and take human life lightly within our national territory under the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun. This is deeply hateful. In order to uphold justice and maintain humanity, we cannot sit idly by. The rickshaw pullers urge the Chen Huizhang Case Support Association to negotiate and strive to achieve the goals of (1) punishing the perpetrators, (2) providing compensation, and (3) ensuring that similar incidents do not happen again. Otherwise, the 100,000 rickshaw pullers in Shanghai will vow to fight to the death. We hope that people from all walks of life will provide strong support. We will not stop until we achieve our goals. It would be fortunate for the rickshaw pullers and the nation. This declaration is hereby announced.

Public Buses Between South Shanghai and West Shanghai to Begin Operation at the End of the Month 150

The Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau's operation of public buses in South Shanghai has been quite successful. The bureau, recognizing the inconvenience of transportation between South Shanghai and West Shanghai, plans to open a new route from Ninghe Road in the city to Caoxi. The route has been determined and station signs have been installed. The original plan was to start operations as soon as possible to facilitate transportation. However, due to delays in the production of the buses, it will take some time. It is expected that the route will officially open by the end of this month.

Abundant Rainfall This Year 151

Rainfall: 677.6 mm

The Observatory reports that rainfall has been abundant this year. From 00:00 AM on January 1 to 12:00 PM on July 31, the total rainfall has been 677.6 millimeters, which is more than the average for the same period in previous years.

Trading of Salted and Dried Fish Begins Yesterday at the Fish Market; Deputy Manager and Others Advise Cooperation 152

Following the centralized trading of marine fish and freshwater fish at the Shanghai Fish Market, the fish trade, as decided by the ninth joint meeting, began yesterday. From now on, all imported dried fish must undergo first-time trading at the market. Members of the Shanghai Salted Fish Trade Association, including 32 businesses south of the 16th Pier, 21 businesses north of the 16th Pier, and 3 businesses in Wusong, a total of 56 businesses, presented reasons indicating that it would be difficult for them to join the fish market for trading. The market has sent Deputy Manager Zhu Kaiguan, along with Council Director Tang Zan'zhi, to advise salted fish businesses such as Jieshun to cooperate. A reporter from New Voice News learned that 25 salted fish businesses are participating in first-time trading. After being advised by the fish market, only two businesses, including Jieshun, have not yet reached an agreement, but generally, there should be no problems, and cooperation is only a matter of time.

Jiawang Coal Mine Company: Multiple Cases Arise Due to Special Compensation; Yuanji and Others File Lawsuits; Plaintiffs Also Lose 153

The Jiawang Coal Mine Company in Xuzhou previously faced economic difficulties and found it difficult to sustain operations. It was then invested in by Shanghai industrialist Liu Hongsheng, who cooperated with the company's former shareholders to reorganize it into the Huadong Coal Mining Co., Ltd. to continue its original business. Subsequently, due to the need for substantial funds to open new mines and construct docks, the board of directors decided to borrow 800,000 yuan from Liu and ordered its former general manager, Gu Zonglin, to raise an additional one million yuan to cover the costs of the two projects. It was stipulated that for each ton of coal produced in the future, a certain amount would be set aside as "special compensation" for those who raised and contributed the funds. This "special compensation" began last year, with funds being set aside and stored. Unexpectedly, this spring, Yuanji and three other former creditors of the Jiawang Coal Mine Company filed a civil lawsuit in the First Special District District Court against Zhang Duchen, chairman of the Huadong Coal Mining Co., Ltd., General Manager Hua Runquan, and all the directors and supervisors, including Liu Hongsheng, Xie Hengchuang, Xu Zhiyi, Bao Zidan, and Li Yuliang, a total of 14 people, requesting that the special compensation be declared invalid and that the defendants be held responsible for rescinding the resolution. While the First Special District Court was conducting the trial, Xie Hengchuang, in his capacity as a shareholder representative of the Jiawang Coal Mine Company, filed another lawsuit against Zhang Duchen, also requesting that the resolution on special compensation be declared invalid. In addition, the company's supervisor, Li Yuliang, filed a criminal complaint against Gu Zonglin and Hua Runquan, accusing them of breach of trust, etc. The dispute over "special compensation" led to both civil and criminal lawsuits. In recent months, the civil and criminal courts have repeatedly held hearings. Zhang Duchen and Liu Hongsheng hired lawyers such as Xu Shihao to present various evidence to prove that there was no violation of the law or breach of trust. The two cases filed separately by Xie Hengchuang and Li Yuliang were concluded a few days ago, and the court ruled that the plaintiffs' claims were dismissed. Only the case filed by Yuanji and the other three parties remained. Yesterday morning, Judge Tao Dejun examined the case and rendered a judgment in favor of the defendant, dismissing the plaintiff's claim. The judgment stated that the plaintiff's claim was dismissed and that the plaintiff should bear the litigation costs.

Daya Film Company: Defrauding Money Using the Name of Ren Chang; Advertising for Tea Servants to Defraud Money; Tao Jianhua and Shen Zhong Remanded in Custody 154

Tao Jianhua, a local resident, 35 years old, recently established the Daya Film Company with Shen Zhong, a native of Qingpu (around the same age as Tao), at 151 Pubo Lane, Luban Road, French Concession. Tao served as the general manager, and Shen served as the general affairs director. On June 25 and 26, they placed large advertisements in various newspapers, seeking actors, actresses, and tea servants. Zhang Jiazhen, a resident of Liuhe, 41 Mofan Village, Gonghe Xin Road, Zhabei, read the advertisement and went to the company to apply. Shen Zhong met with him and offered him the position of tea servant, requiring a deposit of 30 yuan. Zhang then managed to obtain 30 yuan in cash, deposited it in the Shanghai Bank on Baxianqiao, obtained a passbook, and handed it over to Shen along with his personal seal. On July 1, he went to the company to work. On July 4, Shen told Zhang that the manager was in Nanjing and the company needed 20 yuan and asked him to borrow it, promising to return it when the manager returned to Shanghai. Zhang believed him and borrowed the money as requested. After General Manager Tao Jianhua returned to Shanghai, he repeatedly demanded the money back, but Shen Zhong had been avoiding him for several days. Zhang became suspicious and inquired with the Shanghai Bank about the deposit, only to find that the money had already been withdrawn. He then realized that Shen and others were setting up a scam and that the company was merely a facade with no real operations. He reported the matter to the French police a few days ago and requested an investigation. Detective Chen Jiuxiang went and arrested Tao Jianhua and Shen Zhong, and seized multiple copies of the company's articles of association, which listed the names of many members of the National Government Committee, court judges, local dignitaries, five well-known lawyers as legal advisors, and one well-known doctor as a hygiene consultant, all of whom were said to be supporters. They were taken back to the police station for investigation. It was discovered that the names of all the people listed had not been obtained with their consent and were fraudulently used for advertising purposes. Yesterday morning, the defendants were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court for trial. Judge Sun Peng presided over the trial. The Police Department's lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, presented the case, stating that the case was a fraud and required further investigation, and requested a postponement. Tao Jianhua testified that he was a sub-landlord and that the name of the general manager of the Daya Film Company was being used by others without his knowledge. Shen's testimony was evasive. The court reviewed the testimony and ordered a postponement for further hearing. The defendants were remanded in custody.

Paramour Li Xiangsheng Abuses Paramour's Son; Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment 155

Li Xiangsheng, a native of Pudong (41 years old), owns a clothing store at 568 Helong Road. Nine years ago, he cohabited with a woman surnamed Huang from Wuxi (42 years old), who had a son from a previous relationship named Degen, who is now 14 years old. Recently, Li Xiangsheng has been beating Degen from time to time, which has been heard by the neighbors. From 1:00 PM on the 29th of last month to 6:00 AM on the 31st, he tied Degen's hands with a leather belt and beat him all over his body with a bamboo pole, causing him to cry in pain. Neighbors Chen Dingsheng, Tang Wenying, and Madam Chen Li went to persuade him to stop, but he ignored them. A Chinese constable from number 1539 arrived and saw Degen's hands tied with a leather belt. After inquiring about the situation, he arrested Li Xiangsheng and his wife and took Degen with them to the Yangshupu police station, where they were detained separately. Degen was sent to the Sacred Heart Hospital, where it was determined that he had the most severe injuries on his back and left cheek. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The Public Works Department's lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, presented the case and requested a trial. Constable number 1539 and witnesses Chen Dingsheng, Tang Wenying, and Chen Li testified to what happened. Degen showed his injuries, which were severely bruised. Li Xiangsheng testified that Degen had stolen things and eaten watermelon, but his testimony was evasive. Li Huang stated that her former husband was also surnamed Li and that Degen was her biological son and that she did not participate in the beating. Judge Xiao Bianfen sentenced Li Xiangsheng to six months imprisonment and acquitted Li Huang.

Consumption of Tobacco and Alcohol: Over Seven Million; Value of Tobacco Imports is the Highest; Over Nine Hundred Thousand in Imported Foreign Liquor 156

According to the Datong News Agency, the total value of imported tobacco and alcohol in the country for the first six months of this year is quite considerable. The details are recorded below:

Value of Tobacco Imports

The total value of imported tobacco for the first six months of this year was 2.88 million gold units, equivalent to over 6.51 million yuan in national currency. Among them, tobacco leaves were valued at over 2.35 million gold units, and cigars and cigarettes were valued at over 100,000 gold units each. In addition, there were also considerable imports of other tobaccos and cut tobacco. Compared with the same period in previous years, the total value of tobacco imports, in terms of customs gold units, has decreased by slightly more than 10%. However, when converted to national currency, it is still higher than the same period in previous years. Among them, the increase in cigar leaves is more significant, while cigarettes have decreased. The main source of imported foreign tobacco is the United States, reaching over 2.5 million gold units.

Value of Alcohol Imports

The total value of alcohol imports nationwide for the first six months of this year was over 400,000 gold units, equivalent to over 910,000 yuan in national currency. Compared to previous years, this is a decrease of one-tenth. The largest imports of foreign liquor are beer (mostly from Japan), grape juice wine (mostly from France), whiskey (mostly from the UK), and gin (mostly from the UK), each reaching tens of thousands of gold units. Imports of Japanese sake and brandy have decreased sharply in recent years. The total combined value of imported tobacco and alcohol is over 7.42 million yuan.

Twelve-Year-Old Child Peddles Red Pills; Confesses Origins and Destinations; Arrest of Fugitive Wanted Criminal 157

French police detectives Qin Youyu and Zhou Bingcheng, and officers Wu Wengang and Ma Yizhi, saw a twelve-year-old boy looking panicked on the afternoon of the other day (July 30) at the intersection of Albier Road. They stopped him and found a tin of red pills, totaling 1,000 pills, on his person. According to his confession, he was instructed by someone inside the stove shop at 108 Route Lafayette to deliver them to an old man inside lane 1 of Route Pichon. The detectives rushed to number 8, Tongji Lane, Route Pichon, and arrested Zhang Afu. They then went to the stove shop at 108 Route Lafayette and arrested Ye Hansheng, also known as Wang Tianbao. According to the confessions of Zhang and Ye, the red pills were manufactured by Xu Shaogen and "Little Ma Pi." Yesterday, Zhang, Ye, and the child, along with the red pills, were sent to the Second Special District Court. Judge Chen presided over the trial. At the request of the police lawyer, the hearing was postponed for further investigation and to apprehend the fugitive wanted criminal. The court briefly questioned the defendants and ordered a postponement for further investigation. The defendants were remanded in custody.

A Man and a Woman Attempt Suicide by Love; Ingesting Burnt Ends of Cigarettes Causes Nausea; Rope Around Neck Remains Conscious 158

Ren Zhicheng, a native of Ningbo, 19 years old, is an apprentice at the Huixia Silk Weaving Factory at numbers 13 to 17 Huaiying Lane, Taopeng Road, Hudong. Zhang Rongmei, a 23-year-old woman from Taizhou, works at the factory. She is already married and is considered attractive. Because Ren Zhicheng and Zhang Rongmei worked together day and night, they developed affection for each other. Soon, they had a closer relationship. However, Ren was also already married. Moreover, there were many eyes and ears in the factory, making it difficult to be open about their relationship. However, it was soon exposed, and they were ridiculed by their colleagues. Ren Zhicheng was afraid that someone would make trouble. Therefore, on the evening of the other day (July 30), he secretly accompanied Zhang Rongmei to the Shenzhou Hotel at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Fuzhou Road, renting room 218 for a rendezvous. At that time, they paid a room fee of three yuan. However, Ren was only an apprentice and had no large sums to spend. After only a day and a night, they were running out of money. They wanted to leave but could not, and their desire for pleasure could not continue. Not knowing what to do, they suddenly had a strange idea. Yesterday morning, around 11:00 AM, they both swallowed dozens of burnt ends of cigarettes, pretending to commit suicide. Shortly after, they used hemp rope around their necks to simulate hanging themselves. However, Zhang Rongmei, after swallowing the burnt ends of cigarettes and feeling the rope around her neck, felt her heart pounding and became nauseous, vomiting repeatedly. At that time, the waiter on the floor heard the sound and thought it was heatstroke. He hurriedly pushed open the door and saw the two lying on the bed with hemp rope around their necks, pretending to hang themselves. He was greatly shocked and immediately reported it to the police and removed the rope from their necks. Soon, an ambulance arrived and took the two to the hospital. After examination, it was discovered that they had not ingested any poison and their minds were very clear, just like ordinary people. After questioning them, they told the truth, hiding their mouths, which was truly an amusing story.

Flour Exchange Announces Increase in Margin, Cancels Public Warehouse Delivery, and Collects Opinions from All Parties 159

The Flour Exchange issued an announcement yesterday stating: (1) Effective August 1, the margin for August futures trading will be set at 500 yuan per 1,000 bags. The margin for September and subsequent months will remain at 250 yuan per 1,000 bags. This is hereby announced. (2) The trading of January futures next year has been temporarily postponed as the approval from the Bureau of Social Affairs has not yet been received. This is hereby announced. Another announcement stated that the proposal by shareholder Zhang Weiyun and others to cancel public warehouse delivery had been transferred to the board of directors for gathering opinions from all parties and handling the matter accordingly. As this is a major issue, whether the delivery of January futures next year will still be in accordance with Article 71 of the Business Rules, which recognizes factory warehouse receipts, or whether public warehouse receipts will be used for delivery, will depend on the board of directors gathering opinions from all parties and deciding on a method before making a further announcement. This is hereby announced.

Peng Zhou is Kicked by Her Husband; Small Intestine Ruptures and Dies; Police File Public Prosecution; Court Orders Fixed Date for Verdict 160

Peng Shouzen, a native of Yangzhou, owner of a go-between shop at 738 Huade Road, had a verbal dispute with his wife, Zhou, a native of Gaoyou (26 years old), over family matters on the morning of the 21st of last month. In a fit of anger, Peng kicked his wife in the lower abdomen, causing her to fall to the ground in pain. He hired someone to take her to the Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but after her condition improved slightly, he had her carried back. She died at 11:45 PM. The Yulin Road police station sent detectives to arrest Peng and sent him to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention. The deceased was examined by the prosecutor at the Peilun Road autopsy site. As the cause of death was unclear, the forensic doctor was instructed to perform an autopsy. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Bianfen continued the trial in the Third Criminal Court to determine the cause of death. It was determined that she died of a ruptured small intestine and peritonitis. Peng Shouzen's testimony was evasive, denying that he kicked her in the abdomen and claiming that she fell down the stairs and was injured. He requested an assessment. Judge Xiao ordered that he remain in custody and set a date for the verdict.

Exchange, Using Transaction Notes According to Law 166

The Shanghai Exchange Federation received a notice from the Ministry of Industry, Commerce Department No. 45983, stating that all buying and selling done by exchange brokers should use transaction notes in accordance with the law. In addition to the ministry notifying the association to instruct all exchanges and broker associations to comply, such transaction disputes involving the non-use of transaction notes are related to the judiciary. After consulting with the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Justice and Administration replied, "Transactions without transaction notes are not in accordance with the Exchange Law. Courts handling such lawsuits, unless the transaction is deemed legally invalid or has grounds for rescission, should first order the broker to issue a transaction note before proceeding with the trial. The Shanghai Jiangsu High Court's Second and Third Branches have been instructed to comply." The association is hereby notified to inform all exchanges and broker associations. Special notice, July 27, 25th year of the Republic of China, Minister Wu Dingchang.

Medical World 173

Hongkou Epidemic Hospital Busy with Clinic The Hongkou Epidemic Hospital at the north end of Xiangyan Bridge, Yucai Road, Hongkou, has been expanded by the sponsorship of local gentlemen and merchants, Honorary Dean Zhu Jingjing and Feng Bingnan, for ten years. It provides diagnosis and treatment day and night, and hospitalization is free of charge. Every summer and autumn, the expenses for three months require 7,000 to 8,000 yuan, which is all obtained from donations. The poor and sick in that area have benefited greatly. Since the clinic opened on June 20 this year, the number of consultations has reached 13,026 by the end of July. In addition to 2,243 cholera vaccinations, most patients suffered from acute gastroenteritis. There were also 491 hospitalizations. A total of 34 patients were critically ill and rescued with saline injections, with good results. Since the opening of the clinic, only one person has died from the severity of the disease. It is expected that the number of consultations this year will be more than 25,000, an increase of about onefold compared to the 10,198 consultations in the 77 days of the clinic last year. Therefore, the medical director of the hospital, Zhu Xiaofang, and doctors Lin Chunshan, Ni Yushi, Shan Huimin, Zhu Wenjun, Lu Songya, and Chen Chuanren, are all extremely busy.

Chen Daming Opens Pediatrics Hospital Dr. Chen Daming is a Doctor of Medicine from McGill University in Canada and holds a British medical license, license number 1474. He also holds a medical license from the British Columbia province of Canada. He has served as the director of the pediatrics department of Montreal Public Hospital in British, Canada, and the director of internal medicine and surgery, and diabetes at the British Royal Queen's Hospital, the former medical consultant of the Chinese Cuban Legation, and the doctor of Shanghai Xianshi and Yong'an Life Insurance Company, and the president of the Chinese Sanatorium. He came to Shanghai two years ago and set up a clinic at No. 287, East End, Laoba Road, with outpatient hours from 10:00 AM to 12:30 PM and 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM every day, treating all kinds of children's diseases, with very effective results. He then established a pediatric hospital at No. 140 Xiangde Road at the end of Sigota Road, with outpatient hours from 8:00 AM to 9:30 AM, and consultations from 2:00 PM to 3:30 PM, which is a great gospel for sick children.

Dr. Ma Liang's Clinic Relocates German doctor Ma Liang has extensive experience in internal medicine, surgery, and especially in smoking cessation. His clinic was originally located on North Sichuan Road. Now, for the convenience of patients, it has been relocated to Yonghe Pharmacy, No. 105 Guizhou Road, behind the Xinxin Company.

Weather Report 175

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the area around Shandong and the middle reaches of the Yellow River would be clear and cloudy, with northeast to southeast winds. The upper reaches of the Yellow River and the upper reaches of the Yangtze River would have showers, with unstable wind directions. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River would be cloudy and hot, with possible thunderstorms and unstable winds. The East China Sea would have rain and strong south winds. The Taiwan Strait would have bad weather with cyclones due to a hurricane approaching Hong Kong from the northwest or north. The center of the hurricane moved to within about 60 miles of 21 degrees north latitude and 116 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM. The winds were fierce. The hurricane over the Pacific Ocean was slowly moving northwest. Its center moved to within about 120 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM. The winds were normal. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in Shanghai was a high of 84.0 and a low of 70.8. On the same day last year, the high was 94.1 and the low was 78.1.

Standardization of National Products and National Psychological Construction (Continued) 176

— Xu Xiaochu

Twenty years ago, very few Japanese people wore Western suits, but now it is very different. Western suits are convenient to wear and easy to express spirit, so naturally more and more people wear them. However, the raw materials for the Western suits worn by the Japanese are all Japanese goods. So wearing a Western suit does not necessarily mean not loving the country, and those who promote domestic goods do not necessarily have to turn back the clock and advise people not to wear Western suits. The most important thing is to quickly find a way to manufacture various Western suit materials. This is just an analogy. All domestic goods can be inferred in this way. Compared with advocating by following the trend, advocating against the trend has very different results. Otherwise, merely using the good name of patriotism to forcibly suppress people's desires and make them use items they do not like, even if it can be effective for a while, it is absolutely impossible to last. If we adopt this method entirely to promote domestic goods, I dare say that we will not succeed in our lifetime. Therefore, taking advantage of the situation, catering to the trend, and pleasing people are all things that domestic goods manufacturers should pay special attention to under the creed of "standardization." Fine and durable goods that cater to the psychology of the times are the basic conditions for sales. And publicity and distribution should not be neglected. I remember seeing a pair of porcelain vases with burned materials produced by Jianhua Company given by Chairman He Jian of Hunan at a friend's house one day. The patterns and colors were very lovely. Another friend wanted to buy them in the city, but unexpectedly, he could not buy them in all the major companies and domestic goods stores in Nanjing Road. Also, in the commodity exhibition hall of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, I saw several kinds of women's cattail fans, which were produced in Ningbo. The coloring was unique and the style was beautiful. In my opinion, this kind of cattail fan must be popular with modern ladies and can be sold in foreign shops. Also, the bamboo mats in Anqing are exceptionally well-made and are by no means inferior to those in Taiwan, and the price is especially low. Unfortunately, they are still not easy to buy in the city. There are countless similar situations, so ineffective publicity and promotion are also a major shortcoming of those who sell domestic goods. All our domestic goods manufacturers must pay close attention to this point.

The above is all for our domestic goods manufacturers. As for how to correct the Chinese people's wrong psychology towards domestic goods, it is also the most important point in promoting domestic goods. I often hear people say, "Eastern goods are not as good as Western goods. Domestic goods are not as good as Eastern goods." Although it cannot be said that all Chinese people have this mentality, it can be asserted that it must be in the minority. It's really annoying that the more economically capable people are, in other words, the higher the standard of living, the so-called upper class people, the less they use domestic goods, so the sales of domestic goods are mostly in the middle and lower classes. I don't know if it's because the middle and lower classes have insufficient financial resources and simple lives, so they have to use domestic goods in a simple way, or if they have a relatively strong sense of national concept. The most easily seen thing is the cigarettes smoked by the upper class. No matter in Shanghai, Nanjing, or elsewhere, regardless of profession or gender, when you take them out, they are either Gallic, Three Cannons, or Black Cat, Three Five, and Mipanpai. It seems that anything less than this is not enough to show wealth, and it seems ashamed to take out domestic goods such as Baijialong, Good Luck, Beauty, and Golden Mouse. Especially pitiful, for example, the cosmetics displayed in the dressing rooms of wealthy ladies are almost all imported. It seems that displaying domestic cosmetics on the dressing table is indecent, and even if they actually use domestic goods, they only hide them in the cabinet and are unwilling to display them publicly outside. If the behavior of the ignorant and unknowledgeable people is like this, it's still fine, but almost all intellectuals cannot be excluded. Are you sad or not? Chinese people are promoting domestic goods with such "insincerity". I don't know when it will be officially effective.

I think in order to promote domestic goods, on the manufacturer's side, we should (1) strive to improve the quality of goods and adapt to the needs of the times. (2) Pay attention to publicity and promotion. (3) Set up more domestic goods companies and domestic goods exhibitions to provide opportunities for the production community and consumers to come into contact with each other. As for the national level, we should change our wrong ideas, respect domestic goods, and be happy to use domestic goods as a psychological construction for the national promotion of group goods. In this way, the domestic goods industry will flourish and can be expected. And the economic lifeline of the country and the crisis of the national banner can be saved by this. Otherwise, economic subjugation is even faster than military subjugation. I am also a member of the domestic goods business and I would like to encourage you all. (End)

Yesterday at 4 PM: Hitler Declares the Opening of the World Games; Rain Did Not Diminish the Festivities Before the Opening; A Thousand-Person Choir Sang the Olympic Anthem; The Hindenburg Airship Soared Above the Sea of People 177

Central News Agency Special Correspondent, Berlin, 1st: The World Games opened at 3 PM on the 1st in a fervent atmosphere. At 4 PM, German leader Hitler arrived at the venue to participate. The national flags of various countries were raised simultaneously. Athletes from various nations entered the stadium in succession. The president of the Games, Latour, delivered the opening address. At 5 PM, Hitler declared the Games open, raising the Games flag and releasing doves. The torch relay runner who started from Greece also arrived at the venue. Then, athletes from various nations took the oath. At 6 PM, Hitler left the venue, and the grand opening ceremony concluded.

Gas Agency, Berlin, 1st: The 11th Olympic Games were declared open by leader Hitler at 4 PM today. The stands of the stadium were packed with people. The leader and government officials were all around the platform, which was adorned with flowers. Unfortunately, the weather was not favorable, and it started raining around 3 PM. However, the festive atmosphere was not diminished. When a 300-member orchestra and a 1,000-member choir sang the Olympic anthem and entered the stadium, the "Hindenburg" airship soared above.

The 11th Olympic Games opened in Berlin, the German capital, at 4 PM yesterday (around 11 PM local time). The scale of the event, with over 4,800 athletes from 52 countries, was unimaginable. Around 11 PM last night, the Nanjing Central Radio Station, the local Ministry of Communications Radio Station, and a Western merchant radio station simultaneously broadcast the grand opening ceremony, using both German and English. The stadium was filled with thunderous applause and cheers. The Olympic anthem was sung loudly and magnificently after leader Hitler's speech, giving a glimpse of the magnificent occasion.

The Last Torchbearer Arrives

Havas Agency, Berlin, 1st: The Olympic torch arrived at Lustgarten here at 11:35 PM. The Olympic flame was lit in front of the altar in the garden, and Minister of Propaganda Goebbels paid tribute to it, calling it the "Flame of Peace." The crowd cheered. Earlier, at 12 noon, a large group of members of the National Socialist Youth League marched along Unter den Linden to the altar in Lustgarten, where the flame in front of the altar was lit. The garden was decorated with the flags of 52 countries (the participating countries in the Olympic Games), and cheers were endless, creating a very enthusiastic atmosphere. Leaders of the National Socialist Youth League, Schirach, German sports leader Tschammer und Osten, and Minister of Education Rust successively delivered speeches. Finally, the whole venue shouted "Hail Hitler" three times, bringing the torch relay ceremony to a successful conclusion.

National Maritime News Agency, Berlin, 1st: When the last person of the World Games torch relay arrived, the cheers were beyond words. When the torch arrived at Lustgarten, the World Games flame on the altar in front of the Altes Museum was lit. After the ceremony in Lustgarten was completed at 1 PM, members of the Olympic Committee traveled by car to the Prime Minister's Office, where they were personally received by Prime Minister Hitler. Count de Baillet Latour, representing the Olympic Committee, thanked the German Prime Minister for the warm hospitality and the great assistance in preparing for this Games.

National Maritime News Agency, July 31st, Heistendorf telegram: At 11:45 AM this morning, the World Games torch was led by trumpeters and relayed to this place. A Czech runner handed the World Games torch to a German athlete. Customs officials and people from neighboring towns gathered here to witness the arrival of the torch in German territory.

Commemorating the Fallen Soldiers of the European War

Havas Agency, Berlin, 1st: The 11th Olympic Games opened today under cloudy but clearing skies. First, a religious ceremony was held at St. Hedwig's Cathedral, followed by a commemoration at the monument to the fallen soldiers of the European War. Only official vehicles and vehicles of officials were allowed to pass on Unter den Linden and Charlottenburg Street. The streets were crowded with spectators from around 8 AM, eager to catch a glimpse of the dignitaries and athletes from various countries and to wait for the arrival of the Olympic torch. At 9:30 AM, the bells of all the churches in the city rang out, and the religious ceremony began. Afterwards, the flag-bearers of the national teams, along with a battalion of the German Army, two companies of the Marine Corps, and two companies of the Air Force, went to the monument to the fallen soldiers, lining the streets. The audience cheered. Then, the Chairman of the International Olympic Committee, Baillet Latour, accompanied by eleven committee members, the Chairman of the German Committee, Lewald, Minister of Defense General von Blomberg, and the Commander of the Berlin Garrison, General Humbourg, inspected the troops, and Baillet Latour laid a wreath at the monument. The ceremony was completed.

National Maritime News Agency, Berlin, August 1st: The first task of the Olympic Committee members today was to gather at St. Hedwig's Church and the Berlin Cathedral. At the same time, two companies of the Army and one company each of the Air Force and Navy marched in formation on Unter den Linden, followed by 1,800 members of the International Sports Observation Group and members of the Youth Camp. This honor guard gathered in front of the War Memorial. Members of the International Olympic Committee, led by Count de Baillet Latour, inspected the troops and members of the Observation Group. After the inspection, they paid tribute to the War Memorial by laying a wreath.

Havas Agency, Berlin, 21st: The current Olympic Games are scheduled to open here tomorrow. Germany is making every effort to prepare. According to the impressions of general visitors, the achievements of the Germans' painstaking efforts surpass all previous Games. The city of Berlin is decorated with flags and banners, and the traffic is many times busier than usual, creating a festive atmosphere that overwhelms the city. The scale of the Olympic Village and the stadium, in particular, is vast, and the facilities are far more complete than those of previous Games. The Games venue includes a track and field stadium, swimming pool, soccer field, hockey field, polo field, tennis court, equestrian competition field, and indoor sports facilities, such as a fencing hall, boxing ring, wrestling arena, and weightlifting hall, each with its own dedicated space. As for the Olympic Village, athletes from 52 countries are housed there. The village also has an open-air theater with a capacity of 20,000 spectators and a tower that is 76 meters high, which is also a famous building.

National Maritime News Agency, Berlin, August 1st: When countless foreign guests got up from their hotels or apartments at dawn, they found that Berlin had changed its appearance overnight. Every household was flying the flags of all nations, and flagpoles were erected on the main streets. Starting from the Victory Avenue, this festive road, from Alexanderplatz, through Königstraße, the Palace Square, Unter den Linden, out of the Brandenburg Gate to the stadium, was decorated with flowers, and flags of all nations flew in the air. Each flagpole was decorated with dark green and gold ribbons.

Our Country's Representative Wang Zhengting Raises the Issue of the Far Eastern Games Dispute; The Japanese Representative Immediately Declares That an Understanding Has Been Reached; The Proposal of Mr. Wang Was Not Accepted at the Meeting; The Next Games Will Be in Tokyo 180

Central News Agency Special Correspondent, Berlin, 31st: The International Olympic Committee held a meeting on the 31st. As a result, it passed a resolution with 36 votes against 27 to hold the next Olympic Games in Japan. Our country's representative, Wang Zhengting, voted in favor. According to Mr. Wang after the meeting, he hopes that the people of the country will intensify their training within four years so that they can achieve good results in the next Games.

Domei News Agency, Berlin, 31st: The 300th meeting of the Olympic Committee, a subsidiary, was held at 10:30 AM here at the Adlon Hotel. Chairman Latour asked the committee members of various countries to decide on rules in their own countries to curb the abuse of the Olympic emblem. At this time, the Chinese representative, Mr. Wang Zhengting, suddenly requested to speak, explaining the process of the Far Eastern Games dispute and the national stadium, and hoping that the Olympic Committee would resolve this issue. The Japanese representative, Count Soejima, replied that he and Mr. Wang Zhengting had reached an understanding and would resolve this issue through personal agreement before the start of the Games. Therefore, the committee did not adopt Mr. Wang's proposal. At 11:40 AM, the chairman announced a break. All committee members attended a luncheon hosted by the sports officer until the meeting resumed at 3:05 PM and decided on the location of the next World Games.

Domei News Agency, Berlin Special Dispatch, 31st: The Olympic Committee continued its meeting today and voted to decide the location of the 1940 Olympic Games. As a result, with a ratio of 36 votes to 27, it was decided to hold the Games in Tokyo, Japan.

Voting Process

Domei News Agency, Berlin, 31st: A fierce situation unfolded when the Olympic Committee's third-day meeting decided on the location of the next World Games. Before the vote was taken, Japanese representative Kano stated that Japan does not insist on the Winter Games. Then Chairman Latour declared that the vote would be taken. At the same time, the staff distributed two voting papers to the representatives of each country, one printed with "Tokyo" and the other with "Helsinki." Each representative took the one they wanted to vote for, sealed it in an envelope, did not write their name, and handed it to the chairman. British Committee member Barrett counted the votes, and Mr. Latour reported the number of votes. As a result, Japan won the location of the Games by a difference of nine votes. Amid applause from the whole venue, Mr. Kano stood up and made a simple speech of thanks. Finnish representative Crogius celebrated Japan's victory in a solemn manner. Other committee members shook hands with the representatives of both Japan and Finland.

Japanese Residents Celebrate

Havas Agency, Berlin, 31st: After the International Olympic Committee announced this afternoon that the next Olympic Games would be held in Tokyo, hundreds of people from various countries, including 35 Japanese journalists, surrounded Mr. Kano, the chief Japanese committee member, and congratulated him. When the Japanese residents here heard the news, they were all overjoyed and immediately decided to hold a large-scale celebration tonight to mark the occasion. They also told everyone they met on the streets that Japanese sports have made great progress in recent years, and the decision of the International Committee is a reward that the Japanese people deserve.

Kano's Remarks

Mr. Kano, the chief committee member of the country, recently stated that Japan has always upheld the spirit advocated by the ancient Greek Olympic Games and the Olympic Games. However, the location of the modern Olympic Games has been limited to countries in Europe and America. As for Asian countries becoming the host of the Games, Japan is the first. This is truly gratifying. The purpose of the Olympic Games is, of course, to promote sports first, but there is also another great purpose: to bring the people of all countries closer together. We Japanese will do our best to show foreigners the true spirit of Japan. At this time, I am extremely happy. What I can say is that Japan is not only proud of this honor, but also grateful without limits. I also believe that this move will greatly contribute to the idea of international peace.

Chairman's Remarks

The Chairman of the International Committee, Baillet Latour of Belgium, also told our reporter after the committee meeting that "the committee members of all countries present at the meeting expressed great sympathy for both Japan and Finland, who were competing for the host of the next Games, and did not show any bias towards either side. Therefore, the formation of this resolution was not easy. However, the majority of the committee members believed that holding the next Games in an Asian country would promote the true spirit of the Olympic Games to faraway places. This is one of the reasons for Japan's victory. I now congratulate the country and am confident that it will organize the 12th Games in accordance with the traditional spirit of the Olympic Games and be up to the task. In the future, when a certain northern country is the host of the 13th Games, I know that the relationship between Europe, America, and Asia in sports will become even stronger."

Finland Disappointed

After hearing about this meeting, the Finnish delegation also told our reporter that Finland has no choice but to obey the decision of the International Committee. We congratulate Japan on this honor. However, we cannot help but say that the International Committee's decision is unfair to Finland, because Finland has been devoted to sports for 25 years. Recently, the mayor of Helsinki, Mr. von Frenckell, has already made a request to hold the Games in Helsinki in 1944.

The year 1940 is the 2600th anniversary of the founding of Japan. Holding the Games in this special year is especially commemorative. All Japanese people should make this Games the most meaningful in order to promote the progress of national sports and promote the strengths of the national character." Various Aspects of the Olympic Games (II) 184

— Jiang Huaiqing

(II) Meaning

Pierre de Coubertin, the reviver of the modern Olympic Games, explained the original intention of the Olympic Games as follows:

"The restoration of the Olympic Games, under the conditions of modern life, gathers the people of the world together once every four years. The competition of peace and courtesy can organize the supreme form of internationalism."

"Above all, to preserve in competitive sports the noble and heroic qualities that have made people outstanding in the past, and to enjoy in the educational status of today's people the same admirable status as that made by the ancient Greek people's education."

"Competition is gradually spreading all over the world, and it has replaced the unhealthy entertainment and harmful wandering of youth. People in society must have their special shortcomings. True competitive sports can eliminate their evils and promote a healthy national spirit."

"It is difficult to judge to what extent the Olympic concept has progressed, but judging from the various aspects of its inception, its definition is very clear: (1) to create and enhance the friendly relations of peaceful communication between civilized countries; (2) to clarify and eliminate the selfish and fraudulent means in competitive sports, to seek games that everyone can get a fair judgment, and to make competition not use victory as the joy of youth."

"In short, the World Olympic Games has the goals of social education and morality: in the social aspect, it enables people to have a spirit of understanding each other. In the educational aspect: (1) to develop physical education to an active and rational development; (2) to establish public playgrounds. In the moral aspect: (1) the spirit that sports should have; (2) the movement of the masses. In short, to protect and promote pure amateur sports. Dedicated people over the years are there."

Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup: Initiated by Mr. Hu Xiansheng 190

Mr. Qiu Feihai, a famous tennis player from our country, unfortunately passed away last month. The news of his death has caused grief in the sports community. Mr. Qiu represented our country at the Far Eastern Games and various competitions in this city, making outstanding contributions internationally. He spared no effort in promoting tennis within the country. Mr. Hu Xiansheng of the Tennis Committee of the Sports Association has initiated the Qiu Feihai Memorial Cup to commemorate him. It is hoped that enthusiastic individuals will provide support. The proposed measures by Mr. Hu are recorded below:

Purpose: To commemorate the honors Mr. Qiu Feihai has won for our country in this city and other places over the years, his personal sportsmanship, and his significant contributions to raising the level of tennis in our country.

Cup Donation: A large silver cup should be donated by an individual, organization, or through joint effort, with a silver or sandalwood base added.

Competition Nature: The detailed rules for the International Tournament will be formulated separately. The winner's team name will be engraved on the cup. Trophies and souvenirs will be raised separately. The trophy will be kept by the championship team for one year, and this will be replicated annually. When there is no space on the cup base for engraving, other measures will be determined.

Organizer: The National Sports Advancement Association will host the event, or the donating party may designate the host organization.

Competition Date: Either this year or next year, to be determined jointly by the cup donor and the host organization.

The Cercle Sportif Français Tennis Club will invite Japanese student tennis players to perform at the club's court on Route Cardinal Mercier at 4:00 PM this afternoon.

Double Tenth National Scout Review and Camp 191

Preparatory Office Established, Wang Shijie as Director

The China Boy Scout Association, in order to decide on holding a national scout grand review and camp on the Double Tenth this year, deeply felt that the affairs were numerous and the responsibilities were significant. Therefore, on July 7th, it hired the highest responsible officials from the Party and government agencies in the capital to hold a meeting at the Association. Those present included Ye Hanzhang (representative of the Ministry of Communications), Gu Zhenglun, Wang Guqing, Zhu Jiahua, Sun Jiaqi (representative of the Ministry of Health), Yuan Yeqiu (representative of the Beijing Municipal Party Headquarters), Zhang Yiqing (representative of the Ministry of Railways), Lin Huaisang (representative of the Mausoleum Management Committee), Chen Lifu, Lei Zhen, Gu Shusen, Zhao Fansheng, Liu Yongyao (representing Yang Kejing), Ma Chaojun (representing Chen Zuping), Chen Jianxiao, Wang Shijie, Qiu Zhusan, etc. The "Preparatory Committee for the Second National Grand Review and Camp of the China Boy Scout" was announced to be established on the same day. The organizational regulations were passed, and Minister of Education Wang Shijie was elected as the chairman, with Chen Lifu, Zhu Jiahua, Gu Zhenglun, Ma Chaojun, Gui Yongqing, Chen Jianxiao, Yuan Yeqiu, Liu Yongyao, and Lin Huaisang as standing committee members. Chen Lifu was appointed as the director of the Preparatory Committee office, and Liu Yongyao and Lei Zhen were appointed as deputy directors. The Preparatory Committee office was established on July 20th. The office has six groups and one committee: Review Group, Camping Group, Guidance Group, Propaganda Group, Public Affairs Group, General Affairs Group, and Economic Committee. Each group is subdivided into sections and units to manage all matters pertaining to their respective groups. Each group will establish its sections and units in stages, depending on the urgency of the matters, to actively prepare.

Education and Culture Subsidies for Border Provinces 192

The Ministry of Education has decided on the allocation.

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 1st) The Ministry of Education has decided on the allocation of 500,000 yuan for education and culture subsidies to border provinces for the 25th year. The beneficiaries are 13 provinces, including Guizhou, Yunnan, Gansu, Kang, Qinghai, Ningxia, Suiyuan, Xinjiang, Chahar, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Hunan, and Tibet. The use of the subsidies for each province has been designated, and instructions have been issued to the respective provincial education departments to comply. In addition, the Ministry of Education plans to implement an education plan for Mongolians, Tibetans, Muslims, and Miao people this year, which includes ten items such as training teachers, establishing primary schools, social education, production education, compiling textbooks and literacy textbooks, secondary education, domestic study subsidies, fundraising, guidance funding, and precautions. Instructions have also been issued to the respective departments and bureaus to implement accordingly.

Enrollment in Spring

(Nanjing, 1st) The Ministry of Education announced the regulations of the Preparatory Committee for the National Central Vocational School of Industry and appointed Wei Yuanguang as the director of the Preparatory Committee, with Lu Enxu, Shi Zhiren, Du Dianying, Ma Jie, and Chen Mingru as members. Xue Guangqian Obtains Doctorate in Italy 196

Mr. Xue Guangqian of this city, a graduate of the Law School of Soochow University, has worked in Party and government agencies and the banking industry for many years. Last spring, he went to Italy at his own expense and entered the Royal University of Rome, majoring in political economy. He studied with Professor Stanford, the head of the Department of Political Science at the university (Professor Stanford was the former Minister of Finance of Italy, the mastermind behind the financial reform after the Fascist Party came to power, and is currently a member of the Supreme Council). This summer, with Professor Stanford's recommendation, he took the doctoral examination. He ranked among the top in each of the four subjects. The professors praised him highly. He then submitted his doctoral dissertation, which was unanimously approved by all thirteen professors of the university. They praised it for its in-depth research and accurate argumentation, calling it a rare work in modern times. He was awarded the highest score and a doctorate. The dissertation was officially published by the Institute of Political Economy of the university to be widely disseminated. Mr. Xue's dissertation topic was "A Comparative Study of the Banking Systems of China and Italy." It is reported that the examinations were all oral, and there were two debates after the dissertation, one on how to rescue the Chinese rural economy and one on how to promote friendly relations between China and Italy. He argued with the professors from both positive and negative perspectives. Mr. Xue was fluent in Italian and spoke clearly. The audience was deeply moved. After the examination, all the professors shook hands with Mr. Xue and wrote inscriptions for him as souvenirs. Mr. Xu Xingchu, who graduated at the same time as Mr. Xue, also had excellent grades. It is reported that Mr. Xue and others are the first Chinese students to be awarded a doctorate by the University of Rome in Italy. Their success in the examination not only gave the Italian academic and cultural circles a deep impression, but also brought great honor to Chinese students studying abroad.

Dr. Sun Liang Returns to China 197

Lawyer Sun Liang went to the United States last autumn to study the American judicial system. After arriving in the United States, he studied American constitutional law, criminal law, insurance law, and other subjects with famous professors such as Willis, Robinson, and Sutherland at Indiana University. This summer, he completed his studies with excellent grades and was awarded a Doctor of Juridical Science degree by the university. Mr. Sun's article "The Theory of Legal Prediction and Judicial Transcendence" has been published in the American Law Quarterly and has been praised by legal scholars. Recently, the Chinese Student Association of North America invited him to serve as the international propaganda editor. Mr. Sun arrived in Shanghai a few days ago.

Finance: Gold Standard Supply and Demand Balanced 201

The gold market was extremely stable yesterday, with only a six-jiao difference. The supply and demand of major players were evenly matched, and the trend was extremely stable. However, with the trend of opening spot positions on the surface, it finally rose by two jiao. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw London rise and the US remain flat. It was said that the market would close near flat after the close, and that forward prices would soften. The Monteray forward silver price was slightly lower by two hao, ranging up to five hao. Exchange rates narrowed and pastoral rates rose. London gold prices remained unchanged. The standard gold price was still quoted at 1128.60 yuan. In pre-market trading, Shengyuan Yong entered, but Tongtaichang, Dadecheng, Dafa, and Yong all sold. The opening was slightly lower. After the opening, the demand and supply of major players were balanced, and it was extremely stable. At this time, it hovered around only one jiao and appeared quite sluggish. American Cotton Trading is Quite Calm, Sampin Yarn and Cotton Rise 206

Yesterday, American cotton opened with each month rising by 2 to 8 points. The industry is waiting for the government report to be released. Cotton hoarding bulls are mostly settling, and loans for cotton will not be resold, so short selling is gradually decreasing. Piece Goods: Yarn and Cotton Continue to Fall, Cotton Cloth Market Softens in Futures 207

Yesterday's cotton cloth market saw a significant decrease in new transactions of cloth due to the continued softening of yarn and cotton prices. The market price of the original goods of Japanese yarn factories remained unchanged, but the asking price for September and October deliveries was about two jiao per piece lower. As a result, the industry predicts that the market price of white goods will likely fall back when new cotton enters the market in October. The most popular sales in the market were futures dyed twill flannel. Grains: Flour Rises with Imported Wheat, Actual Sales This Month Are Not Smooth, Market Situation Is Still Flat, and Far-Term Months Rise Again to Equal Limit Prices 208

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, each month showed another rise. Starting from the 9th, it rose again to the limit price of the Social Affairs Bureau. The current rebound in the market is purely affected by the rise in foreign wheat prices. Because the previous day's price quoted Chicago up 4-5 jiao, Canada nearly up 1.12 yuan, and far up 6-7 jiao to 1 yuan. Yesterday's price quoted Chicago continued to rise by 1-2 jiao, Canada nearly down 8 points, and far up 4-6 jiao. Therefore, after opening prices, people inside and outside the industry were excited and immediately raised prices by 1-2 fen. The actual sales of this month were slightly weaker, and the highest price was once 3.11 yuan, but then it was slightly flatter. September to November deliveries opened within the limit price.

Because sellers are restrained and buying is quite strong, all prices opened at the limit price. The initial price for December was 3.21 yuan, and then there were not many transactions and the price did not change. Because the limit price for January has not been removed, it has not been sold. The subsequent situation is that if foreign wheat falls back, the market atmosphere will be able to relax, otherwise it may become a stalemate again.

Wheat Futures Market Stable, Spot Wheat Special High-Quality Goods Are Good for 3-4 Fen 209

Yesterday's wheat futures, after opening in the morning, the market in each month was stable. Therefore, most of the customers' goods are sold to the exchange, and there is no lack of long and short chips, so people's hearts have also become stable, and the market is also calm. The rise is only 1-2 fen. Compared with the flour situation, the two are often out of sync. Spot wheat prices, because the prices of standard flour wheat have improved, special high-quality goods are quoted higher by 3 fen, and the medium-grade goods are as usual. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway factory opened at 4.6 yuan for wheat, and the Zhongguan goods were 4.4 to 4.5 jiao. It is reported that Japanese merchants also bought 500-600 tons of special high-quality goods and Zhongguan goods, and the price quoted was 5 fen higher than that opened by the factory.

Oil Market: Sesame Oil Market Rises and Then Falls Back 213

The sesame oil market, after opening at 24.5 yuan, was once affected by the sharp rise in raw materials, and the market immediately increased to 27 yuan. In the middle of last month, Bengbu oil reopened at 27.5 yuan. Afterwards, due to the high price, sources poured in, and the market price fell to 27.2 yuan. Then, because the merchants saw that the inventory was gradually increasing, they were hesitant to move. After half a month of no transactions, 140 to 150 dan of Nansu Prefecture oil were sold yesterday, and the price was only 26 yuan, a sharp drop of more than 1.2 yuan compared with the previous price. It was purchased by local retailers. It is currently found that the inventory of sesame oil from various routes in the city is still about 20,000 cans, accounting for more than 5,700 dan. If sales are flat in the future, the market situation seems likely to continue to fall.

Silk and Tea: Zhenmei Tea Plunges by 15-16 Yuan 214

Since the outbreak of the war in western Morocco, the sales of Chinese green tea have suddenly become sluggish. Tea merchants from Britain and France are mostly taking a wait-and-see attitude. According to reliable information, the current situation is that the transportation and sales of Chinese tea to Europe and Africa are not hindered much, but the insurance premium has been increased compared to before. After days of brewing, the market price of Zhenmei green tea with road village drawn cores has been reduced to 112-113 yuan, a drop of 15-16 yuan compared to before. The other items such as needle eyebrows and pearl tea have also fallen by 4-5 yuan to 7-8 yuan each.

According to the report of the Tea Warehousing Industry Association, green tea has been clearer this week than since the market opened. Various Zhenmei teas have been bought less because various firms dislike their quality, with a total of 4,800 boxes transacted, and the selling price has fallen by about 6-7 yuan compared to before. However, pumping Zhen is still active, and 1,400 boxes have been sold, and the price has also fallen by 5-6 yuan. Although the price of small needle eyebrows has remained stable, there are not many transactions, and a total of 2,800 boxes have been transacted. Yesterday, Zhongzhuang Zhenmei Tongfu and Xiehe each bought a small amount at prices of 73-76 yuan. Gaozhuang Tunwu Zhenmei Baitouhang continued to buy in 300 boxes at prices of 103-112 yuan. Chouxin Xiehe and Jinlong jointly bought more than 400 boxes at prices of 102-115 yuan. Pingshui tea Xiaoxiang Dabang Huacha bought Qiaoyu and Jinlong bought Xiandeng each. A total of 10 bangs have been transacted this week, and the wholesale price is slightly lower than before. Zerose Zhu tea sold 3,000 boxes, and the price is still stable.

Special Feature: My Views on Income Tax 219

— Hai Fan

The origin of income tax lies in England. The time was 1798, implemented to cover the war expenses of the Anglo-French War. Subsequently, the United States, in 1861, due to the Civil War, enacted the United States Income Tax Law. Germany, in 1920, also adopted income tax due to the post-war financial straits. France began just before the outbreak of the Great War in 1914. Italy began in 1864, shortly after the establishment of the Empire. Russia started in 1916, amidst huge war expenditures and declining tax revenues. Japan, also due to naval expansion and the necessity to reduce the Hokkaido product tax, resolutely adopted it in 1887. Other countries such as the Netherlands, Switzerland, and Austria-Hungary also implemented it successively. Although there were changes in the process, the primary motivation was to cope with wartime economy and financial reforms or difficulties. Today, the advancement of income tax has become global. Its amount accounts for a significant proportion of national revenue. An examination of the percentage of income tax to total tax revenue in various countries in 1932 will make this clear.

Given the importance of income tax in revenue, it is not that our country did not pay attention to it before. In the late Qing Dynasty, there was a proposal for income tax. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Finance re-submitted the new proposal, drafting regulations in the second year and announcing them in January of the third year. However, due to the broad scope and difficulty in collection, it was not implemented. In the fourth and tenth years of the Republic, detailed implementation rules were announced twice, ordering implementation, but ultimately, due to domestic turmoil, it did not gain authority. In the sixteenth year, the Nationalist Government was established, and it meticulously planned for income tax. In the eighteenth year, the Income Tax Regulations of the third year of the Republic were finally promulgated, and the implementation rules were also revised. However, the result was still ineffective. In recent years, the government, facing financial difficulties, enacted the Provisional Income Tax Regulations of 31 articles in the 24th year and included 5 million yuan of income tax in the revenue section of the general budget for the 24th fiscal year. However, by the end of the year, there were still no results. The above is a brief overview of the history of income tax in our country, which has never been effectively collected. There are several reasons why it could not be implemented, which are listed as follows: (To be continued) Market Price
